Local Court Trying Murderous Traitors 126

During the January 28th incident last year, many rogues and hooligans were willing to be traitors, working for the enemy, while righteous people and warriors also rose up to resist. Therefore, there were occasional killings of compatriots. Wang Bingzhai and others, villagers of Jinjia Lane, Xiangyin Road, Hudong, were willing to be spies for the enemy, carrying out reconnaissance and transportation work for them. There was a river in the area, and Wang built a wooden bridge to facilitate the enemy's progress. It was discovered by Quan Baogen, Xu Shengqing, Cai Yaoxiang, Xu Jinfu, and others, who went to the bridge at night and tore it down. Wang Fuzhai and others, being supported by the enemy, lay in wait and shot and killed Quan Baogen. After the area was quiet, Wang fled, while Xu Shengqing and others were arrested on suspicion by the local court. It has now been confirmed by the captain of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau's Reconnaissance Team that Wang Bingzhai and Jin Guoting (also known as Ma Pi) were actually traitors who committed murder. Detective Hu Kuisheng was dispatched to arrest Wang Bingzhai and arrest Jin Guoting to be investigated and dealt with. Wang Bingzhai has now confessed, so the local court has filed a lawsuit. Yesterday, Judge Zhu conducted a preliminary investigation and ordered them to be returned to custody to await further interrogation of the remaining accomplices.

Puffer Fish Roe Causes Death 127

Small Restaurant Cooks and Sells Puffer Fish Roe

Three Customers Accidentally Eat It and Cause Disaster

The day before yesterday, Xu Xiaogen from Jiangyin (yesterday's extra mistakenly reported Zhang Da) and his friend Li Zhikui purchased and ate the fish roe at Qian Fuxing Small Restaurant in Guanyinge, and died of poisoning after returning home. The details are recorded below.

Xu's Wife Comes to Shanghai 128

Xu Xiaogen from Jiangyin is currently 51 years old and has always been a dock worker. His home is in the countryside of his hometown. His wife, Chen, has a son named Baolang, who is currently 18 years old and has been an apprentice at Lu Faxiang Garment Shop at No. 148 Tianguanfang, Danfeng Road, Xinbeimen, in this port. Xu Er, because he had not been to Shanghai for a long time, specially took a boat to Shanghai a few days ago. After arriving at the port the day before yesterday, he stayed at the home of his fellow villager Zhu Laoming at No. 70 Dasheng Lane, Xiaodongmen, planning to inquire about his son's recent situation the next day.

Fish Roe for Customers 129

At about 7:00 PM that day, Xu invited his friend Li Zhikui to Qian Fuxing Small Restaurant at No. 34 Guanyinge, Xinkaihe, for dinner. The restaurant was opened by Qian Shouchang from Zhenjiang and has been in operation for four years. The business has been fairly good on weekdays, but all the equipment in the restaurant is simple and crude, so those who go there to eat are mostly coolies. On the morning of the day before yesterday, Qian, tempted by the low price, bought a large batch of puffer fish roe outside and brought it back to the restaurant, cooked it, and put it in large basins on the table for customers to choose from.

Two People Gobble It Up 130

At that time, Xu and others stepped into the restaurant and saw the fish roe displayed on the table, which was bright red in color and fragrant. They ordered the waiter to serve a large bowl (worth 15 silver dollars) on the table, with white rice. The two immediately gathered together to gobble it up. Because the taste was very delicious, they quickly swallowed a large bowl of fish roe and six bowls of white rice into their stomachs. After eating, they settled the bill and left the restaurant, returning home separately. Xu returned to Zhu's house at about 8:00 PM. Seeing that Zhu and his wife, Zhou, were already asleep, he took off his clothes and went to bed to sleep.

Xu Dies of Abdominal Distension 131

Around 11:00 PM, the pain caused by the fish roe suddenly swelled up in Xu's abdomen. Xu suddenly felt as if his abdomen was cut by a knife and woke up in pain from his dream, rolling around in bed. Zhu and his wife were also awakened and got up to check. They saw that Xu's face was pale and his breathing was short. After questioning, they learned that what he had eaten earlier was puffer fish roe, which was poisonous and caused abdominal pain. They immediately called a doctor for diagnosis and treatment. Unfortunately, by the time the doctor arrived, it was too late to save him, and he had already died.

Li Also Dies in Pain 132

Li Zhikui is currently 34 years old and is from the same hometown as Xu. He lives at No. 23 Guanyinge, Xinkaihe. After eating dinner with Xu at the restaurant, he returned home and went to sleep. Unexpectedly, at about 11:00 PM, he also suddenly felt abdominal pain like a绞, and was rushed to Shanghai Hospital for treatment by his friend Chen Wenkui. However, because he had eaten too much puffer fish roe, the fish roe swelled up in his abdomen, and he was deeply poisoned. As a result, he had just arrived at the hospital when he died before being rescued. His body was temporarily displayed at the entrance of the hospital.

Detaining the Restaurant Owner 133

Around 6:00 AM yesterday morning, the incident was learned by the No. 2 Precinct of the First District of the Municipal Public Security Bureau. Director Liu immediately dispatched police chief Li Fuyi and others to investigate at No. 70 Dasheng Lane. Then, they went to Guanyinge and arrested Qian Shouchang, the owner of Qian Fuxing Small Restaurant, and brought the remaining puffer fish roe back to the precinct. After preliminary interrogation by the director, Qian was found to be greedy for profit, selling puffer fish roe, and causing the death of human lives, which was extremely hateful. He was ordered to be detained temporarily, pending verification. Zhou Linshu, the chief of the tenth shop, was ordered to report to the Shanghai Local Court and request an autopsy.

Another Person 134

As for Li Zhikui, who died at Shanghai Hospital, Qin Defang, the chief of the twenty-third shop of the First District, was also dispatched by the director to report to the court and request the dispatch of personnel for an autopsy. However, there were more than just Xu and Li who purchased and ate the fish roe at Qian Fuxing Small Restaurant. However, these diners have all scattered, so it is still difficult to know the exact number of those who have been poisoned. There is also one person who has been discovered. His name is Huang Youcheng, currently 24 years old, also from Jiangyin, who has always made a living by scavenging. After eating the fish roe at the restaurant the night before last, he returned home and felt abdominal pain at 11:00 PM, rolling around on the ground. He was rushed to the Sixteenth Shop Red Cross Nanshi Hospital for treatment. He was said to be severely poisoned and may be in danger.

Robbers Shoot and Kill a Beat Cop 135

Wu Junxuan Killed in the Line of Duty

Injured Robber Apprehended After Pursuit

Yesterday, just as dawn was breaking around 5 o'clock, a shooting occurred at the Jian Dao Qiao (Scissors Bridge) on Huining Road in the South City. A police officer on duty was shot and killed by robbers, and a stray bullet accidentally wounded one of the robber's companions. The detailed circumstances are recorded below. Wu Junxuan, from Tianjin, was 28 years old and a police officer at the Manufacturing Bureau Road police station of the Second District police department. He had only been on duty for six days. This morning, he was assigned to duty at the Jian Dao Qiao position on Huining Road. At dawn, he noticed three suspicious individuals traveling from east to west, talking amongst themselves and appearing fierce. Knowing they were not good people, he ordered them to stop. As he prepared to search them, the robbers, feigning innocence, took the initiative. Two robbers rushed forward and grabbed the officer’s arms, rendering him unable to resist or escape. Another robber drew a pistol from his sleeve and fired, firing five shots, two of which struck the officer. The bullets entered from the upper part of his chest, around the left and right nipples, and exited through his back, damaging his lungs. He immediately collapsed and died. A stray bullet wounded one of the robbers, named Jia (reportedly from Yancheng). The robbers scattered and fled in all directions. A nearby officer heard the gunshots and rushed to the scene. Seeing Jia and his companions running wildly, he knew what they had done and gave chase, pursuing them to the San Guan Tang area, where Jia was finally apprehended. The others escaped. Jia was taken to the Second District police department, where it was found that he was seriously injured. He was immediately sent to Shanghai Hospital for treatment. Police were also dispatched to the scene of the incident, where they recovered five spent bullet casings from the ground. The local Baodi (local security) was ordered to report to the local court, requesting an inquest. Subsequently, a prosecutor arrived on the scene and confirmed that Officer Wu Junxuan had indeed died from gunshot wounds. The death certificate was issued, and instructions were given for the body to be collected and prepared for burial pending further instructions. It is reported that the officer's family, including his elderly mother, wife, and five-year-old son, were all dependent on him for support.

The Revised Draft of the Criminal Procedure Law is Completed 144

The Work of Yu Zhongluo

The National Lawyers Association of the Republic of China, in order to revise the criminal code, resolved to organize a Criminal Procedure Code Revision Committee at a meeting on September 10, 1932. Various proposals were put forward, including the abolition of the prosecutor system and the lawyer interrogation system, as well as the jury system and other important issues. The committee held repeated research meetings, and unanimously recommended that Committee Member Yu Zhenluo be responsible for drafting the main draft. After spending several days, a lengthy draft has now been prepared, consisting of tens of thousands of words. It is currently being printed in two volumes and will be distributed to various committee members within a few days to collect opinions, and then submitted to the judicial authorities for adoption and implementation.

Meida Neirong Store's Failure to Distribute Dividends Leads to Lawsuit 149

| Chen Jianbai Sued by Shareholders |

Chen Jianbai, a shareholder of the Meida Neirong Store at the Huajin Lane entrance on Fuzhou Road, was sued because he failed to publicly distribute the profits accumulated over the years. This led to questioning by his maternal uncle, Bai Puxi, which resulted in a dispute. Although mediation was attempted, Chen overturned the original agreement, so the reconciliation failed. Chen's widowed sister-in-law learned of this and, following Bai's example, demanded a share of the profits. She hired a lawyer and filed a complaint with the First Special District Local Court, requesting that the accounts of Meida and its affiliated company, Meihua, be sealed and preserved, and that further lawsuits be allowed. This was previously reported. It is said that Meida was established in the summer of the first year of the Republic (1912), and the original founders were Chen Ruixiang, Bai Puxi, Ye Shaowu, Ying Zijun, and others. Chen and Bai were uncle and brother-in-law. Chen invested 4,000 yuan, and Bai invested 1,000 yuan. Ye, Ying, and other shareholders invested about 8,000 or 9,000 yuan, bringing the total to 13,000 yuan. At that time, they specialized in military uniforms. However, before long, Ye, Ying, and others withdrew their shares one after another, and the business was run by Chen and Bai. Bai was in charge of internal affairs, and Chen was solely responsible for external affairs. They divided the work and cooperated, and the business grew daily. They then established the affiliated company Meihua. From then on, Chen and Bai each managed one store. In the 19th year (1930), Chen died of illness, and the management of Meida, which he left behind, was taken over by his son, Chen Jianbai. Since then, the accounts have never been made public, and no dividends have been distributed. It was not until last winter that Bai Puxi demanded to see the accounts. Chen also knew that he was in the wrong and asked relatives and friends to mediate, deciding to convert the goods in the store into cash at the actual price and hand over the profit accounts for the past years for distribution. Unexpectedly, Chen went back on his word, and the reconciliation was halted. Chen's deceased brother's wife then followed Bai's example. Now that the court has granted her request to seal the account books, she has taken a further step by having her representative lawyer formally file a lawsuit against Chen.

Bao Inspector Embezzles Red Pills, Then Dares to Entrust Others to Sell Them for Profit 150

Fan Chongxin from Haimen, currently 27 years old, was found on the morning of the 31st of last month at 4:30 AM, carrying 100 silver dollars and 190 paper bills, totaling 290 dollars, alone, walking through the intersection of Route Cardinal Foch and Rue Amiral Bayle in the French Concession. He was spotted by Vietnamese constable No. 167 and two Chinese constables, Nos. 34 and 49, who found his behavior suspicious. They approached, searched him, and found a large sum of money, two ledgers for selling red pills, and a business card of Wang Fusheng, a bao inspector of the French Concession police. When asked where he was coming from, Fan stammered in reply. He was immediately taken to the police station for interrogation. Fan confessed that he was an apprentice and associate of Wang Fusheng, bao inspector No. 148. The money was given to him by Dong Shenshi, the landlady of Dafang Inn No. 20 on Min’guo Road, to be delivered to Wang Fusheng's house at No. 782 on Rue Massenet, and that it was money from selling red pills. The police chief sent detective Zhang Fengming to Dafang Inn to inquire with Dong Shenshi. She stated that she knew Wang Fusheng, but did not know Fan Chongxin, nor had she given Fan any money to deliver to Wang Fusheng. They then inquired with Wang Fusheng, who also claimed not to know Fan, that he was neither his apprentice nor his associate, and that if he committed a crime, he could be dealt with according to official procedures. Detective Zhang, finding no leads, returned to the police station and questioned Fan, who maintained his previous statement. Therefore, Zhang went again to inquire with Dong Shenshi. She then admitted that she had given Fan Chongxin 290 dollars to deliver to Wang Fusheng, but that it was not money from selling red pills. When asked why she had denied it the first time, she claimed that she had forgotten due to being busy. They then inquired with Wang Fusheng again, and Wang also claimed that it was money from a rotating credit association. Zhang immediately reported this information to the Western detective chief, believing that Wang and Dong were indeed suspected of selling narcotics. Wang and Dong were detained. The next day, they were brought to the Second Special District Court for interrogation along with Fan. Wang was ordered to pay 500 dollars in bail, while Fan and Dong were remanded in custody pending investigation. The police have now discovered that Wang Fusheng, bao inspector No. 148, when sent to guard the red pill manufacturing facility broken up on Rue Lafayette near Qianjiatang on March 11th, had actually given some of the red pills to his associate (i.e., Fan Chongxin) to transport out and entrusted them to Dong Shenshi for sale. Zheng Renjun, the coachman of a certain bao inspector who was also guarding the facility at the time, witnessed this. Therefore, yesterday, the witness Zheng Renjun was summoned, and the defendants were brought back to the court. Judge Wu Fanglian presided over the criminal court. First, the police lawyer Yao Zhaodi stated the circumstances of the defendants' arrest and the police investigation, and stated that the police were now prosecuting the third defendant, Wang Fusheng, under Article 357 of the Criminal Code for embezzling items held in official capacity, and the first and second defendants, Fan Chongxin and Dong Shenshi, under Article 6 of the Opium Suppression Law for selling opium substitutes, requesting that they be severely punished according to the law. The evidence, including the cash and ledgers, was presented to the court. The court ordered the defendants to be interrogated separately. Fan Chongxin was interrogated first. He stated that he had known Dong Shenshi for over two months, and had met Wang Fusheng more than a month ago when Wang's child had a full-month celebration and invited him for drinks. The business card on the case was the one used to invite him for drinks. Dong Shenshi had instructed him to deliver the money to Wang Fusheng, saying that it was money from a rotating credit association, and that it was not for selling red pills. Dong Shenshi and Wang Fusheng were then interrogated. Both stated that the money was from a rotating credit association, which had started on the tenth day of the first month of the lunar new year in the year before last, and had dissolved in April of last year due to the war, totaling 48 shares, with 29 installments already paid. They adamantly denied selling red pills. At this point, the court ordered the witness Zheng Renjun to be brought in. According to his testimony, on the evening of March 11th, he drove his boss Zhou Buqui to the red pill facility to guard it. Wang Fusheng later slept in the back room of the living room. In the middle of the night, Wang's associate came and knocked on the door, and after entering, slept with him. The next morning, the associate went upstairs, and he followed him, seeing him grab the red pills from a wheat flour bag and fill two or three of his pockets before leaving. The judge asked if Wang's associate was the first defendant, Fan Chongxin. Zheng turned and examined Fan's face, answering that it was him, Wang's associate. The defense then presented Mi Baoshan, the person in charge of the rotating credit association, who testified about the circumstances of each lottery draw. The court then ordered both witnesses to sign affidavits and then ordered the start of the debate. First, the police lawyer debated, and then the defendants were defended by four lawyers, including Jiang Yiping and Chen Zhigao. The court then declared the debate closed and adjourned the court for a future sentencing.

Verdict on the Case of the Bao Inspector of Guanglu Automobile Company Hitting a Tailor 151

丨Fine of 300 Dollars丨

Xia Jinfu, a shareholder and manager of Guanglu Automobile Company located at No. 60 on Route Paul Beau in the French Concession, was driving a company car with license plate No. 11118 at 4:40 PM on the 15th of last month when he struck and killed Gao Shugen, a tailor, in front of the Zhuangyuanlou restaurant on Rue de la Sœur. The traffic department sent Xia to the Second Special District Court, where he was publicly prosecuted under Article 291 of the Criminal Code for causing death by negligence and Article 7 of the Traffic Regulations for violating traffic regulations. The family of the deceased, represented by lawyer Wang Shizong, filed an incidental private prosecution, seeking compensation of 4,100 dollars. After repeated court hearings, the trial concluded yesterday with Judge Wang Wangxu finding Xia Quanfu guilty of causing death by negligence and fining him 300 dollars. It is reported that the defendant has engaged a mediator to reach a settlement with the family of the deceased, paying 750 dollars.

Guo Weiyi Appeals Lin Yayue 152

丨丨Should Be Made to the Original Trial Court丨丨

Guo Weiyi, a Cantonese who is the chairman and manager of the Guohua Soda Factory, was previously sued in the Second Special District Court by Lin Yayue, a woman from the same hometown, who filed a criminal private prosecution alleging that when she was fostered at Guo's house ten years ago, she was raped by Guo in the bathroom and then continuously for four years, until Guo's wife found out and forced her to return to her hometown, after which she was abandoned and ignored. She requested an investigation. Guo also filed a countersuit against Lin for false accusation. The details of the interrogation have been reported previously. Subsequently, the court ruled that both claims were unfounded. It is now learned that Guo, dissatisfied with the original verdict, filed an appeal with the Third Branch of the High Court a few days ago. The appeal has now been rejected, stating that appeals in criminal cases should be made to the original trial court, as stipulated by the Criminal Procedure Law. Directly filing an appeal is not in accordance with the law, and the original document has been sent to the original trial court for review and processing.

The Absurd Behavior of a Fortune Teller 153

丨Seducing and Raping···Being Beaten···Informant···Drowning Attempt丨

Chou Fengwu, a 31-year-old man from Yancheng, makes a living as a fortune teller, traveling around various places all year round (commonly known as "opening a pier") and residing in no fixed address. A few years ago, he had some savings from working outside, so he took a boat back to his hometown, intending to relax for a while before going out again to pursue his old profession. Xia Qilou, a fellow villager not far from his home, had only two or three acres of poor land, which he and his wife, Fu (named Xiuying), cultivated to make a living. Due to years of famine, the harvest from the fields was poor, making it difficult to survive and causing extreme hardship. Xia was forced to abandon his life as a farmer and go to Shanghai to seek a different livelihood, while Fu guarded the house alone, often facing the risk of running out of food. Chou had known Fu for a long time and, seeing her plight, provided her with financial assistance. Fu, seeing that her husband had been away for a long time without any news, and in addition to Chou's financial help, he also expressed his deep affection for her, leading to a love affair and cohabitation. Xia in Shanghai was unaware of this. Last year, Fu became pregnant. Coincidentally, her husband returned home in the autumn and, seeing his wife's swollen abdomen, became suspicious. He thought to himself that he had been separated from his wife for more than a year, so how could she be pregnant? After several interrogations and inquiries, he finally learned that Fu had been cohabiting with Chou Fengwu for a long time. He was filled with uncontrollable anger and repeatedly punched Chou. However, Chou and Fu were deeply in love and felt a great reluctance to part. Taking advantage of Xia's absence, they secretly trysted from time to time. When Xia found out, he dragged the adulterous couple to court that winter. The result of the trial was that both were sentenced to two months of imprisonment. Xia, seeing that his wife was six months pregnant and about to give birth, pleaded with the court to allow him to take her back under his supervision. Xia then moved his entire family to Shanghai, residing on a small boat owned by his father-in-law, Fu Hengyou, located south of the Outer Rihui Port Railway in this city, in order to sever Fu's ties with Chou. However, Chou, who had been released from prison this spring, learned that Fu had moved to Shanghai with her husband. With his infatuation undiminished, he still tracked her down to Shanghai. Upon learning that Fu had given birth to a son nearly three months ago, he believed that the child was his own and was determined to see his face to fulfill his paternal affection. Recently, carrying his fortune-telling paper rolls and other items, he mustered the courage to barge into Fu's residence, where he was met by Xia and beaten severely again. Chou staggered back home, harboring grievances he could not express, leading him to contemplate ending his life. The day before yesterday, after drafting a complaint and a statement, he boarded a ferry at the Hongkou Port pier at around 5 PM, heading towards Pudong. When he reached the middle of the river, Chou left behind his characters, brush, inkstone, and other belongings, along with the complaint and statement, and then jumped into the river to commit suicide. After his body sank, it suddenly surfaced again and was rescued by the crew, along with his belongings. He was taken to the Second Squad of the Pudong Police, and then transferred to the Third District. After questioning him, District Chief Zhang found his written complaint to be very comical, filled with complaints. It included phrases such as "having spent over 200 dollars on Ying (referring to Fu)" and ended by requesting the Director of the Huangpu River Water Police Bureau to arrest Xia Qilou, whom he called the defendant, and send him to the Shanghai Local Court for punishment. As for the statement, it described the general course of events and stated that he had not served the country by fighting the Eastern dwarfs when he had money, so what face did he have to see the elders of his hometown? He could only hope to be a patriotic general in the next life and destroy the Japanese. After ordering that he be given dry clothes to change into, the district chief ordered that he be handed over to the General Bureau for disposal.

Further Discussion on "Can We Return to the Countryside?" 161

丨Letter from Mr. You Huaigao of the Free Farm on Connaught Road, This Municipality丨

I am a staunch advocate for returning to the countryside and building it up. So, the other day, when I saw the question, "Can We Return to the Countryside?" I was very happy to offer an answer to Shen Bao and a plan for Mr. Xiongsheng. I haven't heard back from Mr. Xiongsheng, but I saw a letter from Mr. Liu Siming refuting me. I admire his enthusiasm and appreciate his concern. I not only want to advise Mr. Xiongsheng, who is interested in returning to the countryside, to go and build it up, but I also urge all college and university students across the country to spend a year after graduation helping the nation build up the countryside. This article has been published in Shen Bao for fifteen consecutive days. I wonder if Mr. Liu has read it? If not, I have a separate print here for you, so Mr. Liu can understand that I am not a "capitalist." Therefore, I not only want to "try," but also to "implement." I not only want to implement it myself, but I also advocate that everyone implement it. Because "trying" means acting hastily without sufficient experience. If the trial goes badly, you have to come back. "Implementing" means that you have studied it thoroughly and are sure of success, and then you implement it. You proceed resolutely, aiming for success. I studied agriculture, practice agriculture, and have not left my agricultural profession for fourteen years. I have personally seen farms in England, America, France, Germany, and Russia. I have interacted with several foreign farm children as classmates. I have spent several months interning in foreign villages. In the more than ten years since returning to China, I have also been to many villages. I have read many books and newspapers about the Chinese countryside. Witnessing the suffering of the farmers, what pains me the most is that the farmers have no education generation after generation. If they had education, there would not be endless natural and man-made disasters, and they would not be so helpless in the current situation. To implement my plan, I must start with cultivating talent. Therefore, I am establishing an institution in Longhua New Field to train rural teachers and agricultural and industrial leaders, which will be established in the autumn. I will also set up several village elementary schools in my hometown of Suzhou. Recently, I have also funded a person to set up a village elementary school in Chen Geng Village, Beixinjing. This is not "trying," but "implementing." In my personal opinion, China's greatest enemy at present is not only the problem of Japanese aggression, but also the ignorance of tens of millions of farmers. Overcoming this ignorance is probably a hundred times more difficult than defeating Japan. If we had education, even if only one percent of farmers resisted Japan, one percent of farmers served as reserves, and one percent of farmers provided supplies, Japan would probably not dare to be so barbaric. The words I dislike the most are saying that people are idealistic and fantasizing. Because these are the words of people who have no ambition, no courage, little knowledge, and a lack of perseverance! Water, fire, and the sky can still be conquered, so how can we not dare to enter the countryside where our food and clothing come from? May Mr. Liu remember the two sentences "The ideal is the mother of fact" and "Failure is the opportunity for success." Unfortunately, most people have no ideals, so there are few facts! Although China currently lacks a paradise, provinces like Hunan, Shandong, Guangdong, Guangxi, Guizhou, and Zhejiang are making great progress in various constructions. (Please refer to the National Education Social Expenditure Statistics Table). China is sixteen times larger than Japan, so the temporary occupation of the three northeastern provinces by Japan and the perennial banditry in Jiangxi do not mean the rest of the provinces are not peaceful and prosperous. Many people such as An Lu Zhong'an, Fang Renlin, Hu Shuyi, Fan Shouyuan, and Ye Guohun are responsible for guidance, and the department's service hours are from 1:00 PM to 6:00 PM every day, located at Nos. 405-406, Silk Industry Building, Shilukou, Sanma Road.

Weather Report 165

Shanghai Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday: The Shandong coast is cloudy, with rain or heavy fog. The wind is tight and comes from the northwest to north. The middle and lower reaches of the Yangtze River are overcast, gradually becoming cloudy, with heavy fog or thunderstorms. The wind is increasing and directionless. The coastal area south of Ma'an Island is cloudy, with heavy fog and southeast winds. The air pressure in southwestern China is decreasing. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the temperature in this city was a high of 81.9 and a low of 60.3. On the same day last year, the high was 52.3 and the low was 42.8.

So I still urge Mr. Xiongsheng to work hard to build his Utopia. I do not advocate Mr. Liu's idea of stopping work to resist Japan and sitting and waiting for victory. My new-style Utopia is a rural standard. Because what is lacking in the countryside is literate and eloquent leaders, so my idea is that urban patriots and people of virtue should go to the countryside to lead farmers to transform and build, and to relieve their suffering. It is definitely not "escaping from the world!" It is "entering the world." Because Mr. Xiongsheng has no place in the city, I advise him to leave the world of the city and enter the world of the countryside. It is completely different from Meng Haoran's seeking plum blossoms in the snow and Tao Yuanming's drinking wine and appreciating chrysanthemums. The new-style Utopia is a village with convenient transportation, scientific production, education, emphasis on hygiene, beauty, and purity. In France in the mid-18th century, there was a model village pastor named Oberlin. He was just as impoverished as Mr. Xiongsheng. He practiced preaching and teaching in the area between Germany, France, and Switzerland, which had long been ravaged by soldiers and bandits and where people's livelihoods were declining. His money was also begged and borrowed, and his food was bread, water, and salt. Through his lifelong efforts, he created his Utopia. There was also a great sacrificer from Belgium named Damiew, who went alone to the most prevalent place of leprosy in the South Pacific Islands to preach and help patients. Sixteen years later, he himself was infected with the disease. Because of his sacrifice, later people actually eliminated leprosy in this place. This righteous man also created his imagined Utopia. I am not a Christian, but I admire their spirit very much. The prosperity of villages in various countries is due to education, and the development and success of education is still due to the willingness of scholars and people of virtue to sacrifice. So I still want to ask Mr. Liu to change his thinking from now on, to be positive and optimistic, and to work hard to advance! The current panic in the United States is because the special markets during and after the European war stimulated the rise of agriculture and industry throughout the United States. When the market changed later, the situation of overproduction today arose. The President is now issuing 200 million yuan in bonds to lend to farmers, and it will soon return to its original state, which is by no means the same as our country's poor countryside. Therefore, Mr. Liu's blaming rural education is completely and fundamentally wrong. American farmers have 120 million yuan in debt, but they still have tens of millions of yuan worth of farmland, houses, cattle, sheep, machinery, and piles of agricultural products. They are just temporarily unable to turn around, not really empty. So please don't worry about American farmers, you still have to design for our country's poor farmers. If Mr. Xiongsheng goes to the countryside, I will indeed help Mr. Xiongsheng solve his personal life, and at the same time, I also hope that Mr. Xiongsheng will do some work in the countryside that will benefit the country and the people. This is the original intention of my publishing "Can We Return to the Countryside?" I hope Mr. Liu will not recognize me as an idealist who likes to sing high tunes, show off, trick people into traps, and enjoy myself. Mr. Liu also said that most of the upper class are snobbish and greedy, while shop assistants and workers are honest and truthful, which is inevitably somewhat arbitrary. You must know that good, evil, wisdom, and stupidity exist everywhere, and you must never use poverty, lowliness, wealth, and nobility as the standard. I said that villagers are relatively honest, which is relative, not absolute. Finally, I still want to hear Mr. Liu's opinion on the "Can We Return to the Countryside?" question raised by Mr. Xiongsheng.

Editor's Note: Regarding the question "Can We Return to the Countryside?" since Mr. You Huaigao of the Free Farm in this city wrote a letter to participate in the discussion, Mr. Liu Simin of this city wrote a letter expressing his opposition (see this column on the 5th and 7th). Now we have received another letter from Mr. You Huaigao, explaining Mr. Liu Simin's questions and listing the reasons for his advocacy of rural education to save the country, which is of great research value. Mr. You also hopes that Mr. Liu will continue to discuss it. Mr. Liu must still have high opinions to express, and we will wait for them.

Important News

General Assembly of the Astronomical and Mathematical Physics Discussion Group Passes Important Proposals from Each Group 167

(Nanjing, 7th) The Ministry of Education's Astronomical and Mathematical Physics Discussion Group continued to discuss in groups on the morning of the 5th. The Astronomy Group passed more than 400 translated names. The Mathematics Group passed several translated names. The Physics Group decided on (1) 7 proposals regarding national defense issues, (2) 2 proposals regarding instrument manufacturing, (3) 3 proposals regarding middle school curriculum issues, and (4) 3 proposals regarding other aspects. At 2:00 PM, they visited the Department of Ordnance Chemistry and Physics Research Institute and the Central Broadcasting Station. At 6:00 PM, the National Compilation and Translation Hall hosted a public banquet for all members. At 8:00 PM, the Director of the Department of Ordnance, Yu Dawei, gave a lecture on weapons. At 9:00 PM, the Mathematics Group continued to discuss and decided (1) to ask the Ministry of Education to set up mathematical research institutes in various universities and to appropriately set up mathematics professorships, (2) to ask the Ministry of Education to reward the publication of middle school mathematics magazines, and (3) to ask the Compilation and Translation Hall to establish a mathematics terminology review committee. On the morning of the 6th, physics and mathematics were still discussed in groups until 9:00 AM. A plenary session was held, attended by 55 people, chaired by Zhu Jiahua, to discuss the proposals of each group, including 3 proposals from the Astronomy Group, 11 proposals from the Mathematics Group, and 16 proposals from the Physics Group. Among them, 7 proposals regarding national defense were all passed. A proposal that astronomy and mathematical physics should cooperate with each other was also passed. The meeting adjourned and closed at 11:30 AM.

This Municipality

Joint Declaration of Universities 170

Urging various schools to organize student unions

Preparatory Committee Reschedules Meeting for Tomorrow

The Preparatory Committee of the Shanghai University Student Union, in order to urge various schools to organize student unions so as to establish the University Student Union as soon as possible and enrich the strength of young people to resist insults and save the country, specially issued an organizational declaration yesterday to inform all students in Shanghai, and scheduled a second preparatory meeting at the Youth Propaganda Team tomorrow (Sunday) at 2:00 PM to discuss all important proposals. The details are as follows:

Organizational Declaration: Today, when internal and external troubles are tormenting each other, the survival of our nation has indeed reached the most critical and serious stage, and the judgment of whether the national destiny will be cut off in the future still depends on the final efforts of all the people. We young students are usually praised as the backbone of society and encouraged to be the pillars of the country. At this time when the disaster of subjugation is imminent, if we do not rise up and be the vanguard of the people, we will not only fail to live up to the expectations of society for young people, but also betray the responsibilities that young people should fulfill for the country. However, the country today is full of dangers, and it is not possible to save this ancient country full of holes and sores in one fell swoop, nor is it enough to sit down and make declarations and just vent "anger." We must persist in fighting and never slacken, and everyone should work from their own positions, taking it as their responsibility to prepare for the enrichment of "strength," so that the country's future can be saved. To achieve this goal, it is impossible to succeed without organizing steps and a sound organization. In view of this, this association initiated the preparation of the "Shanghai University Student Union" so that we can take the same steps and share the same goal, with the spirit of perseverance and hard work, and carry out long-term and effective struggle. It is hoped that all universities in Shanghai, those that have already organized will join this association as soon as possible, and those that have not organized will prepare at an accelerated pace, so that the strength is concentrated and the actions are consistent. The organization of a sound youth group can consolidate the line of defense against insults and save the country. When disaster is at hand, there is no room for hesitation. We hope that all the students of all universities in Shanghai will learn from this together.

Convening of the Preparatory Committee: The second preparatory committee of the association was originally scheduled to be held this afternoon, but due to the problem of the meeting place not being properly contacted, it has been rescheduled to be held tomorrow (Sunday) at 2:00 PM at the Youth Propaganda Team of Xiaoshimen to discuss important issues. Rescheduling notices have been sent out separately.

Shanghai Tutoring School to Open Soon 172

The Shanghai Tutoring School at the intersection of Malang Road and Lafayette Road, Xixi Lane, this city, has been enrolling students since the beginning of this month. Every day, dozens of people come to register. The teaching method focuses on practicality and economy, and the duration is not fixed (tutoring for one month is also possible). The fees are low, only two yuan and four yuan per month. There are also preferential rates for continuous tutoring for three months (the Yijiao group is completely free). It is said that the school will open soon.

Lower Examination Qualifications for Overseas Chinese Children Enlisting in Military Academies 173

The Central Army Military Academy is recruiting enlistees for the tenth term. Previously, considering that the education and culture of Mongolia and Tibet were relatively backward compared to the mainland, the request of the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission was specially approved to lower the examination qualifications for Mongolian and Tibetan students. It is now learned that the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission sent a letter based on the request of overseas Chinese students Zhou Longsen and others, requesting the school to follow the example of Mongolian and Tibetan students and approve the reduction of examination qualifications. This has now been approved by the General Training Department and sent to the Shanghai Central Government for investigation. The Municipal Government specially ordered the Public Security and Education Bureaus yesterday to investigate and handle it.

Academic Lectures 175

At the academic lectures the night before last, Xu Mingcai first introduced the brief biographies of Zhou Zijing and Zhu Maocheng in the first classroom of the Engineering Hall. Then Mr. Zhou gave a lecture on "Report on the Observation of Industry in Shaanxi." Although the speech was recorded, it was requested not to be published. After the lecture, a live-action film was shown, which was taken by Mr. Zhou when he traveled to Shaanxi. It briefly covered the living conditions of the people of Shaanxi, the transportation situation, and the ancient scenic spots and historical sites, which gave us, who live in the blessed land of Jiangnan, a deep impression. Then Zhu Maocheng gave a lecture on "Observations on the Recent World Economic Situation." The insightful remarks stated that the manpower of the entire China is only equivalent to the hydropower generators of thirteen or fourteen frames, showing the weakness of China's national strength. He also used the hat-making industry to describe the reasons for world unemployment. Both solemn and humorous, it was thought-provoking. Mr. Zhou's film used a microscope to observe the situation in Shaanxi, and listening to Mr. Zhu's speech was like looking at European and American countries with a telescope. In a few words, more than 300 listeners were moved.

Regulations for Primary and Secondary School Normal Vocational (10) 177

Article 106: Normal schools shall establish the following two types of committees: (1) Moral Education Guidance Committee, composed of the principal, all directors, all teachers, and the school doctor, with the principal as the chairman, responsible for all guidance of students, and meeting once a month; (2) Financial Audit Committee, composed of three to five full-time teachers elected by the teachers, with the members serving as chairman in rotation, responsible for reviewing income and expenditure accounts and receipts, and meeting once a month.

Article 107: Normal schools shall hold the following four types of meetings: (1) School Affairs Meeting, composed of the principal, all teachers, school doctor, and accountant, with the principal as the chairman, to discuss all matters of reform and innovation in the school, and meeting once or twice each semester; (2) Academic Affairs Meeting, composed of the principal and all teachers, with the principal as the chairman, or the Director of Teaching or Director of Academic Affairs as the chairman in the absence of the principal, to discuss all matters related to teaching, practice, and library equipment procurement, and meeting once a month; (3) Moral Education Meeting, composed of the principal, all directors, all grade teachers, and the school doctor, with the principal as the chairman, or the Director of Teaching or Director of Moral Education as the chairman in the absence of the principal, to discuss all matters related to moral education and management, and meeting once or twice a month; (4) Administrative Affairs Meeting, composed of the directors and all staff members of the school, with the principal as the chairman, or the Director of Administrative Affairs as the chairman in the absence of the principal, to discuss all matters related to administrative affairs, and meeting once a month.

Article 108: The principal of a normal school must be of sound character, excellent talent, and graduated from a normal university, university education college, education department, or other college and department and have studied education courses for 20 credits or higher canonical school, and meet one of the following qualifications: (1) Having served as a teacher, college professor, or full-time lecturer in a national university for more than one year; (2) Having served in a senior position in a provincial or municipal education administrative agency for more than two years and having achieved results; (3) Having served as the principal of a senior middle school for more than one year or the principal of a junior middle school for more than three years and having achieved results.

Article 109: Anyone with one of the following circumstances shall not be employed as the principal of a normal school: (1) Having violated the criminal law and the evidence is conclusive; (2) Having not cleared the handover after serving as a public official; (3) Having achieved mediocre results in serving as a principal or administrative position of a teacher; (4) Suffering from mental illness or chronic illness and unable to serve; (5) Having improper behavior or bad habits.

Article 110: Teachers of normal schools must be of sound character, and the subject they teach must be their specialized subject, and they must have research on primary education and meet one of the following qualifications: (1) Having passed the normal school teacher examination or qualification; (2) Graduating from a national or foreign normal university or university education college education department; (3) Having graduated from a national or foreign university undergraduate, higher normal undergraduate, or specialist course and having more than one year of teaching experience; (4) Having graduated from a national or foreign vocational school or specialized school undergraduate and having more than two years of teaching experience; (5) Having published valuable specialized works; (6) Having refined skills (specifically applicable to labor teachers).

Memorial, and at the same time, invited the President of the Conference, Li Zhaohuan, to drink a glass of champagne together to enhance friendship. After the visit, they returned to Rong Hong Hall for dinner, and Wang Zhengting and others gave speeches during the dinner, which ended at 2:00 PM.

Shanghai County Improved Private School Promotion Week 179

From April 10th to 15th

Participated by Party and Government Organs in Each District

The Shanghai County Education Bureau, according to provincial orders, has designated April 10th to 15th as Improved Private School Promotion Week to improve private schools. The measures have already been determined and are extracted as follows:

Promotion Dates: (1) Dates: From April 10th to 15th, 1933 (2) Zonal Promotion Dates: Zone 1, April 12th; Zone 2, April 11th; Zone 3, April 10th; Zone 4, April 13th; Zone 5, April 14th; Zone 6, April 15th.

Participating Organizations: Each district party headquarters, district office, township office, elementary school, social education agency, and organization will take on the responsibility. The presiding organizations are: Zone 1, Minhang People's Education Center; Zone 2, Tangwan People's Education Center; Zone 3, Zhuanqiao Agricultural Education Center; Zone 4, Sanlin Agricultural Education Center; Zone 5, Chenhang Elementary School; Zone 6, Maqiao Agricultural Education Center.

Promotion Objectives: (1) The improvement of private schools does not emphasize negative bans, but rather active improvements; (2) The improvement of private schools must make the private school curriculum achieve the same practical results as short-term elementary schools and simplified elementary schools; (3) The improvement of private schools must ensure that the school buildings are well-lit and ventilated; (4) The improvement of private schools must ensure that all private school textbooks use reviewed and approved textbooks; (5) The improvement of private schools must improve teaching methods, should be divided into group teaching, focusing on explanation and application.

Promotion Methods: (1) Hold promotion meetings to lecture on the significance and methods of improving private schools; (2) Distribute or post various promotional materials for improving private schools; (3) Convene township mayors for a discussion meeting; (4) Organize propaganda teams to go to various villages to hold public lectures and masquerade performances on improving private schools; (5) Send a letter to the county party headquarters to publish a special issue of the Shanghai People's Journal on Improving Private Schools.

[Amateur First Division]

Our Country's Pellet Gun King Li Gongying Achieves a Major Victory 182

Defeats Nie Kaoer and Advances to the Second Week

Result: 1000 Points to 546 Points

In the first week of the Shanghai Amateur First Division Pellet Gun Competition, our country's Pellet Gun King Li Gongying showed his true colors yesterday, defeating Nie Kaoer with 1000 points to 546 points. Mr. Li once held hegemony over Shanghai two years ago, but in the previous two sessions, he was defeated by Mei Dina. Mr. Li's ambition to avenge himself and win the championship remains the same as before. Yesterday's opponent was too weak, and his victory was as easy as turning his hand. From now on, he advances to the second week, and his future is limitless. During the first ten shots or so, Nie Kaoer also briefly ranked above Mr. Li. However, the good times did not last long, and he was soon left behind, with no chance of turning the tables. In the first half, Mr. Li led with 500 points to 291. In the second half, Mr. Li scored almost every shot, with a maximum score of 74, and scored above 11 points many times. Compared with his past performance, this is not his best record. Nie Kaoer's technique was very steady, and under pressure, he remained calm and composed, fighting as usual. His defeat was not due to lack of effort, but due to insufficient strength.

Spring and Autumn

Golden and Silver Ham Hock 196

— Zhan Lu

This joke was heard at a banquet. One Miss Yi, who is admirable, simply delivered a blow to those stuck in unrequited love.

Miss Yi was returning home from school. She took the ferry at the pier outside Xumen, paying a copper coin to get to the other side, which shortened the journey considerably. That day, a young man was standing on the bow of the boat, and intoxicated by her beauty, he stared at her without blinking. This was extremely dangerous! Suddenly, a small steamboat emerged from the arch of Wanniang Bridge, and the once calm river surface was instantly stirred into rough waves! The young man standing on the bow lost his footing and was about to fall into the heart of the waves when a jade-like arm suddenly reached out and held him tightly. He was saved from falling into the water with a splash.

After landing, the young man tearfully thanked her for saving his life. She only smiled slightly and left in haste. Later, the young man hoped to meet Miss Yi again, but he heard that she had transferred to a school in Hangzhou and there was no chance of seeing her again. The young man was already married, but his wife was not as beautiful as Miss Yi. Therefore, he longed for her beautiful face day and night, and became a lovesick wretch! The cure for lovesickness was only to meet Miss Yi, and if she did not come, he would wither away and die! The young man's mother and wife were filled with endless worry. They heard that Miss Yi was returning home for spring break, so they went to her door to beg her to visit the patient. Just her willingness to come and see the patient would greatly improve his condition.

Miss Yi, feeling a sense of compassion, actually came to visit the patient. With each visit, his illness lessened. On the third visit, the young man was already able to get out of bed. Miss Yi said, "I will come again in three days to inquire about his condition. When I come, I will personally cook some delicacies to help the patient regain his appetite." When the young man heard this, he was moved to tears again.

Three days later, Miss Yi, as beautiful as a goddess, came. The delicacies she had cooked were braised ham hocks, one red and one white, commonly known as Golden and Silver Ham Hocks. The young man had a high appetite, and with the "gift from a beautiful woman," he could of course eat heartily and greedily. However, she wanted the young man to distinguish the taste of the two ham hocks. First, she had him close his eyes tightly, and then she gave him some of the golden ham hock and asked, "How does it taste?" The young man said, "Very good." Then she gave him some of the silver ham hock and asked, "What about this?" The young man said, "Also very good." She asked him tightly, "Are there two different tastes?" The man replied, "Just one taste."

Suddenly, her delicate jade-like hand delivered a palm strike to his face! Then, in a clear, oriole-like voice, she scolded, "Since you know that the ham hocks don't have two different tastes, how can a woman have two different tastes?" With that, she left without looking back.

At that moment, the young man's face turned dark and pale, almost like the golden and silver ham hocks. His lovesickness was cured from then on. The cure for lovesickness only required a single dose of prickly pear.

The characters in the play include elegant young masters, flower-like young ladies and wives, merchants, lawyers, prostitutes, stars, beggars, poets, students, movie queens, generals, gentlemen, and hooligans...

Recent performances include patriotic fervor and grief in the face of national crisis, the passionate rush to save the country, tearful love, and the twisted, bizarre, and ugly aspects of seduction, abandonment, rape, and debauchery. There are...

Before the world is destroyed and the cities collapse, this grand theater will continue to present its creations.

Wedding 197

— Jian Chonglou

I have not tasted the experience of a wedding, whether old or new.

But whenever I watch relatives and friends hold weddings, I always see the same routine; "The bride and groom stand awkwardly in the middle of the hall, as if waiting for legal judgment. Then, the officiant delivers a long speech about the talented man and beautiful woman being a perfect match, followed by the marriage host saying a few polite words of forgiveness. Then, the guests who are good at speaking deliver speeches, and in front of the men and women, they say inappropriate things like 'working hard' and 'intensifying the production of citizens.' Then, the guests laugh as if they are watching a Charlie Chaplin film! Finally, the bride and groom bow to express their gratitude, and this embarrassing wedding comes to an end."

The MSG of Life 198

— A Jie

What is the meaning and flavor of people living in this world? This "mystery" is probably solved thoroughly by very few. Do we live to eat? Animals also do that. Do we live to reproduce? Animals also know how to mate. Do we live for wealth and status? In the end, very few achieve their goals! Even if they do achieve their goals, the wealthy are probably more worried than the poor. Do we live for money? A person cannot live forever, and no amount of money can buy a fence on the ocean floor. Tao Yuanming said it well, "Life is not a hundred years, yet we harbor a thousand years of worry." This is the point. So, is life without any "meaning" or "flavor?"

Each person has their own "view of life," which is each person's "meaning" and "flavor" of life. Therefore, society inevitably has many disputes, and the world is full of trouble. For example, the Japanese have a view of life based on venomous snakes and beasts; they find cruelty and viciousness the most flavorful. The Chinese have a view of life based on pigs and snails; they find stupidity and weakness the most flavorful. Or they have a view of life based on aphids; they find greed and self-interest the most flavorful. Or they have a view of life based on mice; they find timidity and fearfulness the most flavorful. Tastes differ, and appetites vary. Therefore, there is more than one kind of "view of life."

Stupidity, fear, weakness, deception, selfishness, arrogance, luxury, and ease are the favorite delicacies of the Chinese appetite, and they are also like the MSG of life. With the above virtues, life is not boring, and the body and mind feel comfortable. Isn't this making them the MSG of life? How can it be known that the Japanese use aggression, attack, cruelty, and fierceness to season their cooking? This kind of MSG is very meaningful in life. The nature of the MSG added to food is fundamentally different, so "national character" also differs.

We are born in China today, a country with internal and external troubles. First, we must fundamentally change our tastes and change our appetite. Quickly use "bravery," "frugality," "public spirit," and "righteousness" as the MSG of life. We should find it extremely flavorful to eat, able to strengthen our muscles and bones, increase our wisdom, and become a great nation in the world. We must never use "stupidity," "fear," "selfishness," "arrogance," "luxury," and "debauchery" as the MSG of life!

Northeast Fourth Regiment Commander 200

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Three: In the End, Failing to Untie the Bell, He Went to the Door and Made a Mistake, Secretly Pitying the Girl's Hair Knots; Wishing to Share Food with Others.

Old Man Zhao said, "I don't believe in saving money. What would I do with it? Would I take it to the coffin with me? You go now, don't waste time in the heavy snow. Hurry up, it's good to get some heat in your body." Zhao Ziqiang agreed and went out. Old Man Zhao closed the storm door and looked out at the snow scene through the glass window for a while, then continued reading his Romance of the Three Kingdoms. When he saw the battle scenes in the novel, he thought to himself, "My son is a company commander. A company commander in a battalion isn't small, but when tens of thousands of people are fighting, the sacrifice of a company commander is simply insignificant." Thinking of this, he couldn't read the novel anymore. From this gate, he could vaguely see the Xiyuan Barracks, so he put on his leather vest and walked towards the gate. Passing by the entrance of the Yang family's courtyard, he heard Guizhi say, "The Zhao company commander and his son in the backyard are really good. When I smell the aroma of this beef, my heart aches." Jiang said, "What are you sad about?" Guizhi said, "Can't I buy two catties of beef and make soup for you to drink?" Old Man Zhao was very touched when he heard this. In the afternoon, the beef soup was well simmered, so he used a pottery bowl to hold most of it and asked Xiaolin to invite Guizhi over. He said with a smile, "Girl, your heart is really kind. I have some soup here. Take it back and give it to your mother to drink." Guizhi said, "Drink! How can that be? This is Company Commander Zhao's filial piety to you, how can we take it?" Old Man Zhao said, "It doesn't matter! Our child can afford beef, but you can only afford radishes. This soup has our beef and your radishes. Considering our strength, the effort we put in this joint venture is about the same. Logically, you should get half." Guizhi smiled and said, "How can you say that?" Old Man Zhao took a step closer and said in a low voice, "You can smell the aroma of beef soup, doesn't your mother smell it? For this little bit, you should take it back for your mother to taste. You need to know: I'm not giving you something to eat, I'm just helping you fulfill your share of filial piety." These words moved Guizhi's heart, so she half-squatted and gave Old Man Zhao a bow, and said with a smile, "Then thank you." After saying that, she took the bowl of beef soup away. This bowl of beef soup, however, aroused a newly emerging plan in Jiang's mind. The joys and sorrows of life, the partings and reunions, are always like this, originating from a little thing. (35)

Shanghai Night Talk 202

— Zhang Ruogu

Spanish Dancer

In the shop window on the street, there is a photo of a woman wearing a long skirt with a cluster of fresh flowers in her hair. What appears before me is Asuncion Granados, a Spanish dancer and pipa virtuoso, performing at the Summer Pic Theater. Tickets are priced at five yuan, three yuan, and two yuan, on April 3rd, 5th, 7th, and 11th, at 9:15 PM. There are also a few lines in English.

Looking at the large evening newspaper in my hand, I know that tonight is the second performance of this famous dancer. While I was pondering, a man in black clothes came across diagonally and turned his head to say:

"Ah! Mr. Shaw!"

"Oh! Mr. Zhang!"

"How have you been?"

"How have you been?"

"Where are you going?"

"Nothing, just taking a walk on the street, waiting to see the 'Ah Sad Heart, Granada Peach' dance in a little while."

"How coincidental, I'm also planning to go."

"That's great, I've already bought two tickets. I'll give you one."

"What? Aren't you going with your wife? Then I won't be polite and will gratefully accept it. Thank you."

At 9:15, Mr. Shaw and I were sitting in the Summer Pic Theater. My number was H11, and the ticket stub was printed with Stalls S5.00.

Looking up, the stage was a dull black curtain, with two gold AG letters on the left and right, surrounded by a garland of auspicious grain. Below were women from Greek mythology, either dancing or playing music. In the left corner was a triangular-tailed black grand piano, completely like a memorial service scene, with only a portrait of the late Prime Minister or martyr missing in the center.

A Spanish man in a snow-white shirt and black evening dress came out, not a presenter. As soon as he sat down at the piano, I knew it was the pianist Jose Serrano. After the overture, a young girl in complete Spanish attire jumped out from behind the curtain. Her charming face, graceful posture, enchanting eyes, and gorgeous clothes were even more alluring and moving than the photo printed in the advertisement. In two hours, Granados performed eighteen solo dances. The dance moves and costumes were different for each dance. She is not like the jade-legged dances commonly seen on the screen. If you want to appreciate the rhythm of the music while her body is dancing, or want to smell a strong fragrance when she is sweating profusely from dancing, then you might as well go see Duncan or Tanixiang, the two dance stars. Granados cannot perform these two characteristics.

This night, I saw a program completely in Spanish for the first time in Shanghai. This Spanish dancer and pipa virtuoso performed a total of eighteen programs. Among them, "Spanish Serenade", "The Afflicted", El Delirio, etc. were the best.

Ah Sad Heart, Granados's only advantage is her pair of beautiful and flexible arms. She holds two wood-like Spanish special instruments, striking a series of crisp sounds. When struck rapidly, the sounds deeply hammer at your heartstrings. In the dim blue light, when she is spinning and dancing, her pair of bare arms move up and down like two white carp eels swimming and jumping, which can make you dizzy. When the dance reaches its climax, her long skirt spreads out like an opened umbrella, revealing a pair of snow-white and tender bare shanks, which can make people's hearts beat faster. The more she dances, the more excited she becomes. Occasionally, the wide skirt will fly to her waist like a balloon, and under the skirt, the pink shorts without leg pipes are faintly visible. Someone in the audience shouted Bravo, and she also sent an enchanting smile.

Granados has a thick waist and a bulging belly, which are two major shortcomings that cannot be improved. Also, she likes to wear high-heeled leather shoes when wearing long skirts, and she only uses a piano accompaniment from beginning to end. These will detract from her dance skills.

It is expected that Granados is not welcomed by the audience in Shanghai.

New Advances in the Radio World: Vacuum Tubes That Don't Need Filaments 205

— Zhenzhi

The fact that vacuum tubes need filaments is a shortcoming of vacuum tubes. Because with filaments, vacuum tubes have a certain lifespan. Therefore, the method of generating electrons by using ionized gas has become the goal of radio research. This work has already taken a lot of effort in Germany. What is introduced here is the wireless vacuum tube (also known as cold cathode vacuum tube) recently completed by Dr. Henderson in the United States.

The completed filamentless vacuum tubes have one, two, and three electrodes. As for four, five, six, and seven electrodes, they can all be made in theory. Now, let's explain one type of three-electrode filamentless vacuum tube to illustrate the rest.

The figure on the left is the external shape of the triode, and the figure below shows its internal structure. The bulb is filled with rare gas. A is the anode, and B is the cathode. A circuit is completed with a high-voltage battery and a certain amount of resistor. This resistor is used to limit the current in the tube, otherwise the current will reach an excessive value due to the too low resistance of the ionized gas. Now, connect the battery to the A and B electrodes, and a beautiful arc will occur between the electrodes. The bulb filled with xenon will be pink, and the bulb filled with helium will be purple. This arc is formed by the collision of positive ions and electrons dissociated by the applied voltage. C is a cylinder with many small holes (only one hole is drawn in the figure), which is sleeved outside the arc electrode. D is the grid, and E is the screen electrode. Its function is as follows: the cylinder with positive charge slows down the speed of the positive charge ions, so as not to disturb the electron flow between the cylinder and the screen electrode. Therefore, the grid placed in the middle of the electron flow can completely control the function of the bulb, just like an ordinary triode.

This type of vacuum tube has various functions, such as oscillation, amplification, amplitude modulation, and detection, and can be competent. It is expected that this type of product will be available on the market in a year.

Mineral Radio with Good Selectivity 206

— Cai Guanghua

Everyone knows that mineral radios are easy to manufacture and cost very little. After equipping them, they can be used permanently without spending any more money. What is considered most regrettable is that the sound is too weak and the sound reception is not good. And poor selectivity is also a major drawback. The former simply has no way to improve except by using vacuum tubes, while the latter is relatively easy to solve. Recently, the Popular Mechanics magazine published the manufacturing methods of several mineral radios with very good selectivity. The translator has tried them one by one and feels that the results are not bad, so he has translated them as follows.

(1) Type A Radio丨As shown in Figure A

This is just a mineral radio, and there is nothing special about it. It's just the relationship between the coils. L1 is the primary coil, and La is the secondary coil. They are wound on a bakelite tube that is three and a half inches long and two inches in diameter. Use No. 26 enameled wire. The primary coil is wound 23 turns, and the secondary coil is wound 72 turns. The Cl capacity is 0.00035MFD, and the C2 capacity is 0.001MFD. The dotted line in the figure indicates whether to use it at will, depending on the test results.

(2) Type B Radio丨丨As shown in Figure B

This mineral radio has an extra filter, so the selectivity can be increased, and the capacity of the components is also different.

The filter coil (Trap Coil) is wound on a bakelite tube that is three inches long and one and a half inches in diameter. Use No. 26 enameled wire to wind 94 turns. The capacity of Cl is 0.0005MFD. The primary coil L and the secondary coil L2 are wound on the same bakelite tube that is 21-2 inches long and 41-4 inches in diameter. Use No. 32 enameled wire. The primary coil is wound 17 turns, and the secondary coil is wound 107 turns. The capacity of C2 is 0.0005MFD, and the capacity of C3 is 0.002MED. The first thing to pay attention to is that the mineral radio needs good sky and ground lines. According to the author, when these two radios used exquisite sky and ground lines in Chicago, they had amazing results. From this, we know that the influence of sky and ground lines on mineral radios is not trivial.

Finally, I hope that the comrades who study radio can start with small components. You must know that a radio with more than a dozen tubes is not necessarily interesting. A small mineral radio may also give you a satisfactory hope.

Filter 207

— Qiyao

There are more and more radio broadcasting stations, and the radio waves in the air are becoming more and more complicated. Therefore, an ordinary radio can receive the broadcasts of almost every station on every dial. Sometimes, two stations can be received at the same time, resulting in mutual interference, often disrupting good programs, and there is no way to receive them. The filter can correct this problem and can filter out programs that you don't want to listen to or other broadcasts.

In practice, filters can be roughly divided into three types: the first type is a high-pass filter, which can allow current with a frequency higher than a certain frequency to pass through and filter out those with a frequency lower than a certain frequency; the second type is a low-pass filter, whose function is exactly the opposite of the above; the third type is a band-pass filter, which can allow current within a certain range from a certain frequency to a certain frequency to pass through, and those that are smaller or larger are filtered out.

Filter Construction: It is made by connecting coils and capacitors in series or parallel. The most commonly used filter on radios is shown in the figure. It can reduce the sound of the nearest radio station. The principle is as follows:

Suppose there are two waves with different frequencies FIF2, which induce currents J1I2 in the antenna, which pass through the abcd circuit. When the self-oscillation frequency of the LC circuit is equal to F1, the current Il is the smallest. Because the frequencies of F1 and F2 are different, the LC circuit cannot make F2 the smallest at the same time. In this way, the LC circuit can filter out the current I1 and allow the current I2 to pass through alone.

Making a filter is very simple. First, prepare a hard paper cylinder with a diameter of about 2 inches to 2.5 inches, and wind about fifty or sixty turns of No. 24 insulated copper wire on the outside to form an induction coil; then use a 0.0005uf or 0.00025uf variable capacitor and install it as shown in the figure. Connect one end to the antenna and the other end to the antenna terminal of the radio. The method of use is also very simple. For example, when the dial is at a certain degree, you can hear the broadcasts of both ABI stations at the same time. If we want to filter out the broadcast of station A, then first slowly rotate the dial to make the broadcast of station A match the loudest position, and then rotate the variable capacitance of the filter to make the broadcast of station A the lowest, until it is completely extinguished. In this way, we will not be disturbed by station A when listening to the broadcasts of station R or other stations.

About Power Supply: The Most Economical B Battery Substitute 208

— Pan Renrong

Fans who play DC radios are always troubled by the excessive cost of daily electricity purchases. Here is the most economical B battery substitute. The materials used are as follows. If the power supply transformer can be wound by yourself, the total cost will be about fourteen or five yuan. T is the power supply transformer. The primary is two hundred or one hundred volts directly on the light bulb. The secondary can have two or three. One is a high-voltage coil to supply the plate and grid of the rectifier tube, which needs about two hundred volts. One is a five-volt low-voltage coil to supply the filament of the tube. The rest are reserved for A batteries. As for the design, it depends on the vacuum tube of the radio. V is a vacuum tube with a slightly larger plate current, such as 201, 509, 171, etc. L is a low-frequency choke coil (AudioFrequencyChoke) for filtering, which can be replaced by a secondary low-frequency transformer. C1 and C2 are both two megafarads (MFD) fixed capacitors. C3 is the same, but a capacity of only one megafarad is enough. R is a 40,000-ohm resistor, which can also be replaced by five photovoltaic light bulbs. It is nothing more than reducing the B voltage for the detection stage. The B negative (B·) is best connected to the ground wire, which can reduce the AC noise to a minimum. The high voltage output of this B battery substitute is about one hundred and sixty or seventy volts, so daily three- or four-tube DC radios can be used.

An Economical Power Transformer 209

— Li Yuanqing

丨Can be used for four-tube radios丨

There is a small transformer for electric bells on the market, which is very small in size (4x4x2.5) and sold at a very low price. It is available in electrical material stores everywhere. The primary coil is connected to an external voltage of 200 to 250 volts, and the secondary has two coils (the transformer originally has only three terminals, and you must find a way to separate the two middle terminals during the改造, as shown in the first figure X). One is three volts and the other is five volts. The output power is about five or six watts. Connecting these three transformers together can supply power for a four-tube AC radio.

As shown in the second figure, the secondary coil S1 of T1 is for the filament of the 227 detection tube. (When using, if it exceeds 2.5 volts, a small light bulb can be connected in parallel for illuminating and adjusting the dial.) oS2 is for the filaments of two 201 low-frequency amplifier tubes. S3 of T2 is connected to S5 of T3, and S4 is for the filament of the 171 rectifier tube. If the OB voltage output is too high, you can rotate R to adjust it. oS6 is left unused. For detailed wiring methods, please refer to the second figure.
