Free Talk

Modern History 212

— He Jiagan

From the time I have memories, until now, wherever I have been, in open spaces, I have often seen "magic shows," also called "conjuring tricks."

These conjuring tricks generally only come in two types:

One type involves teaching a monkey to wear a mask, put on clothes, and perform a series of sword and spear routines; riding a sheep in circles. There's also a bear, kept alive on thin rice porridge and already skin and bones, performing some tricks. Finally, they ask everyone for money.

The other type involves placing a stone in an empty box, covering it with a handkerchief from left to right, and conjuring a white dove; or stuffing paper into their mouth, lighting it, and making smoke and flames come out of their mouth and nostrils. Next, they ask everyone for money. After getting the money, one person pretends it's not enough and refuses to perform, while another person persuades him, telling everyone to give five more. Sure enough, people throw money, so they ask for four more, three more...

Once enough money is thrown, the magic show begins again. This time, a child is stuffed into a small-mouthed jar, with only a small braid visible. To get him to come out, they ask for more money. After collecting enough, somehow, the adult uses a sharp knife to stab the child to death, covers him with a bedsheet, and has him lie stiffly. To bring him back to life, they ask for more money.

"At home, rely on parents; away from home, rely on friends... HuazalHuazal," the magician says in a solemn and sorrowful tone, making a gesture of scattering money.

If other children get too close to watch carefully, he will scold them; if they don't listen, he will hit them.

Sure enough, many people "Huaza." When the amount is close to what they expected, they pick up the money, pack up their gear, and the dead child also gets up on his own and walks away with them.

The onlookers disperse in a daze.

The open space is temporarily silent. After some time, this routine comes again. As the saying goes, "Everyone can perform magic tricks, but each has different skills." In reality, it's always the same routine for many years, and there are always people watching, always people "Huaza," but there must be a few days of silence in between.

I've finished talking, and the meaning is very simple, just saying: after everyone "HuazaHusza" for a while, there will be a few days of silence, and then this routine will come again.

Only now do I remember that I wrote the title wrong; this has truly become something that is "neither dead nor alive."

A Stroll in the Deep Night 213

— Lin Huiyin

A street that would be very lively during the day is very quiet at night. The shops on both sides, except for perhaps one or two open all night, are all closed; the sidewalks are crisscrossed with patches of light, now dim, now bright, coming from the poles, from the wires, from the houses, or sometimes, from the moon.

Strolling alone in such a scene will make you think of many things you have forgotten: a glance of an eye, a squeeze of a hand, a shake of a head. However, thinking of all this is like thinking of other people's affairs; the emotions of joy or anger that you felt when these things first happened will not return to you; at most, you will only smile knowingly, your soul and your thoughts understanding each other.

Strolling like this, you will also sink your whole body and mind into empty thoughts, thoughts emptier than empty dreams. You will think that when it dawns, there will be two suns fighting in the sky, or that the earth is already rotating westward; you will think that your soul may have become someone else's soul, or that your body is definitely no longer your own body. You will think of chewing iron, swallowing fire, or drinking all the water in the world, to make people feel the thirst of life.

Sometimes your train of thought will be cut off by the headlights of a car, but even if it is cut off, you will not want to extend it again; or you will no longer remember what you were just thinking, and you will start thinking about something else, or you will simply not pay attention to those headlights, and even if you do pay attention, you will still continue your train of thought. You are no longer your own master; your master is thinking itself.

There are also times when you suddenly feel that someone else is walking in front of or behind you, and you also realize that his pace has been consistent with yours since you don't know when, so you speed up or slow down your pace to make it different from his, and as soon as you see a corner, you turn, so as to start another solitude.

What a stroll in the deep night makes you think of is far different from what you would think of at any other time or in any other situation.

The Origin of a Master (Continued) 214

— by A. Mallrois, translated by Wei Ke

"One hour is enough; and the sad thing is, Grace, this thing can succeed."

"Let's try it."

"But I can't brag."

"Then, my child, whenever someone asks about your background, you may hesitate for a moment, blow a large puff of smoke directly into the questioner's nose, and then say the following very simple sentence: 'Have you never seen a river?'"

"What does that mean?"

"It means nothing," Grace said, "so they will find your words very beautiful. When you have been fully discovered, understood, and praised by them, we will reveal the inside story of this matter and make fun of their embarrassment."

○ ○ ○ ○

Two months later, the preview exhibition one day before the official opening of the Tuoshi Painting Exhibition was completely successful. The beautiful Mrs. Koslesursga, with her sweet and gentle voice and fragrant body, never left her new great man.

"Ah!" she exclaimed repeatedly, "This artistic sensibility, imagination, and power! What wisdom, what revelation! But, dear, how did you achieve such an amazing synthesis?"

The painter hesitated for a moment, blew out a large puff of smoke, and said, "Dear madam, have you never seen a river?"

Then the beautiful Polish woman's lips moved, and she spoke many congratulations in a sweet and gentle voice. The young and famous Lewig, wearing a rabbit fur collar coat, argued in a large crowd: "Really sharp! Really sharp! I have long said that the most despicable thing is to paint according to a model. But, Tuoshi, tell me, where did you get this revelation? Did you get it from my thesis?"

Tuoshi really hesitated for a moment, blew a triumphant puff of smoke into his nose, and then said, "Sir, have you never seen a river?"

"Excellent!" Lewig expressed his approval, "Excellent!"

At this time, a famous day merchant visited the studio, took the painter's sleeve, and led him to a corner. "Tuoshi, my friend, you are really a cunning thing. This can be blown up. Please leave all your works to me. Before I tell you, don't change your painting style, I will sell fifty works for you every year... Is that okay?"

Tuoshi mysteriously smoked, noncommittal.

The studio slowly emptied. When the last visitor went out, Grace went to close the door, and we heard the murmuring praises on the stairs gradually fading away.

The Crossroads of Time and Love 215

— Zhang Ziping

"Where's Lao Cao?"

"He went to Lao Ha's place. Lao Ha sent someone to call him early in the morning."

She answered him with a smile.

"… Mr. Lin, please wait a moment, I'll get some water for you to wipe your face."

"No, I can do it myself."

He said, putting on his outer coat and pants. After putting them on, he got out of bed.

"I'm really sorry about last night."

Hao suddenly blushed and said to him. But he couldn't figure out what was going on. He thought that she hadn't done anything wrong to him last night.

"What's the matter?"

Haiquan asked in surprise.

"That annoying thing, Shiguang…"

She didn't finish her sentence and laughed as if it was very interesting. But Haiquan couldn't laugh at all. He just opened his mouth and stared at her blankly. "…I said, Mr. Lin is here, you shouldn't be so improper, but Shiguang still…"

She blushed even more.

Just as Haiquan was at a loss, he suddenly saw the second landlord's maid sending a letter up from downstairs.

"A letter for Mr. Lin, sent by a child."

Hearing this, Haiquan hurried out of the stairwell and took the letter. He knew that it was written by Tang Yaoxing, because he had told Tang Yaoxing the day before yesterday that he would temporarily use Cao Shiguang's residence as a temporary communication address. His fingertips trembled as he opened the letter and looked at it.

"Demon this afternoon, please participate. Meet at my place at twelve o'clock."

Seeing only the abbreviated word "Demon," his limbs, like his chest, trembled. He thought, is Tang Yaoxing really going to carry out what he said that day? This is not something to be taken as a game. Ah! Danger! Danger!

"That night, I shouldn't have signed the word so confusedly. My heart is exceptionally cowardly. But my mouth said very tough things. Now the day of the test has arrived."

After only the novelist and the painter were left, the novelist quickly put his hands in his pockets and burst into a terrifying laugh. Tuoshi looked at him in surprise. "Look!" My child, Grace said, "Don't you believe we have conquered them? Did you hear the words of that little trickster wearing a rabbit fur collar? And the words of that beautiful Polish woman? And the three young and beautiful girls repeatedly saying: 'So new! So new!' Ah! Tuoshi, I know that the stubbornness of mankind is unfathomable, but such a result has exceeded my expectations."

After he finished speaking, he couldn't stop laughing again. The painter frowned, and when the other party laughed so hard that he couldn't catch his breath, he suddenly said:

"You stupid thing!"

"Stupid thing!" the novelist shouted angrily. "When I succeeded in the most beautiful caricature since Picasso…"

The painter glanced at the twenty analytical portraits with a proud expression and said decisively:

"Yes, Grace, you are a stupid thing. There is something in these paintings…"

The novelist stared at his friend in horror. "This is terrible!" he exclaimed, "Tuoshi, remember. Who gave you the hint of this new painting method?"

So Tuoshi hesitated for a moment and blew out a puff of smoke:

"Have you never seen a river?" (End)

The Hair of the Soviet People 216

— Ke Duo

Now, almost all the modern young ladies, wives, and female students in Shanghai apply rouge and powder, paint their eyebrows, and dye their hair. Of course, delicate eyebrows and loose hair do add a lot of artificial beauty, but it is inevitably too troublesome.

Among women in the Soviet Union, very few use artificial means to embellish their appearance. Women who apply rouge and powder, paint their eyebrows, or perm their hair probably cannot be found in one or two out of a thousand women; and these one or two are only those non-Party and non-League actresses, the wives and young ladies of embassies and consulates, the wives and daughters of foreign technicians and engineers, and the very rare prostitutes who lead stressful lives. They want to win the favor of those they like, so they have to scheme and fight, and dress up in fancy clothes. They are willing to spend even fifty rubles to have their hair done once.

The working women in factories and farms do not have much free time to decorate themselves, nor are they willing to engage in meaningless decorations. The romance of "looking at makeup under the crystal curtain" in a deep boudoir is indeed not easy to find in the Soviet Union. In their spare time, if they don't go to literacy classes, libraries, or cram schools to study, they go to do those physical and mental exercises, such as shooting, swimming, and skating. Soviet men's haircuts are also not like those modern young masters in China who imitate fashionable women and perm their hair into curls. They only need ten minutes to get a haircut when they go to the barber shop. The barber only cuts some long hair, shaves seven or eight times on the left and right cheeks and upper and lower jaws, and simply finishes the haircut procedure. They will never wash their faces, take out earwax, comb their hair, knock on their backs, spray perfume, or apply cold cream for the barber. However, the white cloth around the neck and the brushes used for shaving must be sent to the laundry factory for disinfection after each use before they are allowed to be used again; otherwise, they will be punished by the Health Bureau.

The Financial Community Was Extremely Busy Closing Accounts the Day Before Yesterday 224

The financial community traditionally used silver as the standard. All transactions, incoming and outgoing, were calculated in silver. Foreign currency had to be converted to silver at a fixed rate for accounting. After the Ministry of Finance officially announced the abolition of silver, there was initially a wait-and-see attitude. Although the abolition of the "li" rate was implemented on March 1, silver and foreign currency were still used in transactions. After a delay of more than a month, on April 6 (i.e., the day before yesterday), the Ministry of Finance suddenly issued a telegram ordering the implementation of the foreign currency standard within a limited time. This sudden measure was unexpected by the financial community, so they held a meeting overnight to discuss solutions. Details were recorded in yesterday's newspaper. Yesterday, banks and money shops were extremely busy with the closing of accounts. It was reported that banks such as the Central Bank of China and the Bank of China extended their office hours to midnight to handle the exchange of silver and foreign currency, organize collection and settlement, and change transfer methods. Yesterday, the work was not completely finished, so there will still be one or two busy days.

Securities 225

Public confidence is gradually stabilizing.

Public bonds show signs of continuing prosperity.

A uniform rebound of 45 jiao to 1.2 yuan.

Yesterday at the Chinese Merchant Securities Exchange, the public bond market gradually recovered, showing signs of continuing prosperity. The crisis on Qinhuangdao Island had been resolved, and public confidence in the market was gradually stabilizing. However, there were still sell orders for No. 38 bond and the Northern Syndicate in the morning. The initial prices of each lot rose slightly, and the 20-roll bond even rose by 45 fen. The auction for consolidated salt tax bonds declined by 23 fen, likely due to oversupply. There were continuous sell orders in the second lot, and market prices continued to weaken. Among them, the No. 19 customs bond rose by 2 jiao due to the unique demand for No. 20 bond. The salt tax also rose by 2 jiao due to purchases by the Northern Syndicate. Therefore, the situation in the morning was still chaotic. In the afternoon, rumors spread that the Japanese cabinet was about to collapse, and Araki may not be able to carry out his militaristic policies. Public confidence in the market suddenly turned high, and No. 38 bond had also stopped selling. Therefore, the prices of both lots in the afternoon rose by 12 jiao to 45 jiao, and trading was also more active than in the morning. Most of the buyers were the Northern Syndicate and guest syndicates. The resulting market prices rebounded uniformly by 45 jiao to 1.2 yuan, mostly recovering the losses from the previous day. The future may not decline in the short term. The total transaction volume was 6,722,000 yuan, including 12,000 yuan in spot goods and 6,710,000 yuan in futures, of which consolidated salt tax accounted for 2.8 million yuan, demobilization bonds for about 1.2 million yuan, and the rest ranged from tens of thousands to 450,000 yuan.

Rice Prices in Hexia Continue to Rise by a Few Jiao 233

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, there were over 30 sources of rice, and demand from urban and rural shops and stomachs remained strong. The prices of freshly colored Suzhou Tongbang rice and Nangang rice continued to rise by a few jiao. Due to commission issues, Hakka merchants stopped trading. Tianjin customers intended to deduct 2 jiao and 5 fen, while sellers were only willing to pay 2 jiao and 3 fen. The two sides were in disagreement over this 2-fen commission, so Qingjiao and other thin rice varieties were sold off with no orders. Market prices remained firm. There was a lack of goods for Duyangjian and Yinyuan, and prices continued to rise. Bianyuan sales were slightly active, with no change in prices.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, there were about 20 sources of rice from various routes in Hexia. White japonica rice sales were sluggish, and there was a lack of high-quality rice deliveries. The market was weak by a few fen. There were few thin rice arrivals, and sales were flat, with prices remaining stable. (Hakka Indica Rice) Yesterday, Hakka Indica rice sales in Fujian remained active, with slight arrivals. There were also arrivals of foreign rice. The market remained stable. Recently, Hakka Indica rice arrivals have been strong, further affected by the new arrivals and new prices of foreign rice. Prices have fallen uniformly. (Foreign Rice) Fook Ka Company has been arriving with goods for several days. Old goods from Anli Company are being sold for 8.15 yuan. Flour and Wheat Prices Vary 235

The current month flour market is uniquely popular, with a small difference of half a fen to one fen from later months.

The long-term wheat market is good by 4 to 7 fen, with the current month following closely by one fen.

After the opening of the flour market in the morning, foreign wheat futures and spot prices both rose. In addition to Hakka merchants purchasing spot goods, they also purchased standard near-term contracts, so the prices of near and far months rose uniformly, with the largest increase being about one fen. However, after the rise, factories hedged a large batch of long-term flour, and the market suddenly fell again. Hakka merchants are very active in current flour, and both buying and selling are present in the long term, so the long-term price still fell. The current month, due to the extraction of cash, closed still up 2.5 li, May was unchanged, June was down a small fen, July was down 0.75 fen, August was down half a fen, and September was down a small fen.

The wheat market presented a swirling situation in both the upper and lower markets. However, the standard wheat has been changed to a foreign currency standard. In the future, orders with foreign merchants must also be calculated in foreign currency. Traders generally believe that after foreign firms take the foreign currency standard, they must raise prices to sell, so they all intend to purchase. The foreign wheat telegram rose by 34 jiao, and the spot price also rose by 35 fen. Furthermore, due to the rise in gold prices, the exchange rate increased even more. Therefore, in the long-term closing, September was up 7 fen, August was up 4 fen, July was up 5 fen, and the current month had some goods arriving to hedge, following closely by only one fen. Yesterday, the Grain Exchange changed to the foreign currency standard, and the above-mentioned price increases are all calculated in foreign currency.

The North-South Goods Industry's Method for Abolishing Taels and Changing to Yuan 236

The North-South goods industry implemented the abolition of taels and change to yuan on the 6th. Therefore, the industry association specifically convened a temporary meeting yesterday to discuss and decide to comply with the order to switch to the foreign currency standard from today onwards. For previous incoming and outgoing funds that were traditionally calculated in silver, in addition to converting to foreign currency at the legal rate of 715, future incoming and outgoing transactions will all be based on the foreign code standard. All rules remain the same. The following is a revised foreign code, which was previously strongly opposed to using the four-舍-六-入 method for converting silver to foreign currency at a rate of 715:

One Qian and Two Fen One Jiao and Seven Fen Three Qian Four Jiao and Two Fen

The above sales are traditionally quoted in yuan

Ministry of Industry Plans to Establish National Paper Mill 251

Establish Pulp Mill in Wenzhou

Establish Paper Mill in Shanghai

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Industry plans to establish a national paper mill. After sending personnel to Wenzhou to investigate raw materials, the investigation results show that the bamboo produced in Wenzhou is indeed suitable for papermaking raw materials. However, the area lacks high-altitude hydraulic power and cannot use water to generate electricity. It has now been decided to build the national paper mill in Shanghai. A pulp mill will be established in Wenzhou to specialize in manufacturing papermaking raw materials for shipment to Shanghai. The total capital amount is set at five million yuan, to be jointly funded by the government and merchants. The government is raising more than two million yuan, and three million yuan will be raised from the business community. The Price of the German National Revolution 261

Reuters, Berlin, 7th Chancellor Hitler announced to the public today that the German revolution had resulted in the deaths of 330 people, injuries to 40,000 people, and unemployment for 100,000 people in the business community. This is the price of Germany's recovery. Among the listeners were cabinet members, diplomats, and news reporters.

Restoration of the Awarding of Medals 262

The German government is currently discussing the restoration of the honors, medals, and awards that were abolished by the Weimar Constitution, to be awarded by President Hindenburg. The first type of medal will be awarded to those who have contributed to the national revolution, followed by medals for art and science.

Unification of National Administration 263

A new law was promulgated today, under which each state will have an administrator appointed by the central government who will have complete control over the state cabinet. The administrators are subject to Hitler's control. Hitler himself is already the administrator of the state of Prussia and is expected to appoint Deputy Prime Minister von Papen or Speaker of the Reichstag Göring as the Prime Minister of Prussia. The new law makes state elections unnecessary.

Havas, Berlin, 7th The German government plans to implement the system of the former provinces of Alsace and Lorraine (now belonging to France) before the European War in all states to promote the unity of the federation. According to the government plan, each state will lose its "state" status and become a "region" of the federation. Each region will be ruled by a governor who is only subject to the central government and has the power to appoint and dismiss the administrative heads of each "region" (i.e., the current state prime ministers). Hitler will appoint himself as the governor of the state of Prussia. Once this plan is implemented, the internal affairs of Germany will be thoroughly unified, and the autonomy that each state has been striving to maintain will be eliminated.

Dentsu, Tokyo, 8th The impact of the decision to retain Minister of Justice Oyama on the political situation is highly valued by all parties. Although Prime Minister Saito tried his best to persuade the Minister of Finance to stay after visiting the Yuen Palace on his way back from visiting the Grand Shrine, the Minister of Finance is respecting the tacit understanding with President Suzuki of the old year and his intention to resign is even firmer today. Stimulated by the Oyama Minister of Justice issue, he will definitely submit a formal letter of resignation to Prime Minister Saito within the day. On the other hand, if Prime Minister Saito has no hope of dismissing the formal resignation of the Minister of Finance, he intends to replace him. However, the reorganization of the cabinet may not proceed as easily as the Prime Minister intends, especially since the military and the Seiyukai cabinet members have already expressed their absolute opposition to replacing the Minister of Finance. Therefore, the resignation of the Minister of Finance makes it difficult for the Prime Minister to clean up the situation. It is expected that the Saito cabinet will still have no choice but to resign en masse at this time.

The Seiyukai Temporarily Observes (Dentsu, Tokyo, 8th) Minister of Education Hatoyama visited Suzuki, the President of the Seiyukai, at his private residence at 2:00 p.m. yesterday to report on the events before and after Minister of Justice Oyama submitted his resignation, and at the same time, he had a conversation about the issue of his own advancement and retreat, and left. Then, he visited again at 9:00 p.m. to discuss everything, and it was unanimously agreed that since the red issue under the jurisdiction of the Ministry of Justice has been returned to Minister of Justice Oyama's resignation, the same responsibility issue of Minister Hatoyama under the jurisdiction of the Ministry of Education is naturally also affected. Therefore, Minister Hatoyama's solo resignation at this time is a useless act. As a result, it was decided that the current cabinet would have to resign en masse in May, so the Seiyukai will not take active action at this time, but will temporarily observe the development of the political situation in a self-respecting manner.

Dentsu, Tokyo, 8th Regarding the resignation issue of Minister of Justice Oyama, the Seiyukai issued the following statement: It is a matter of course for the Minister of Justice to submit his resignation, and Prime Minister Saito actually requested its return when he made his report. Those who promote the current cabinet's determination to consolidate and cling to power, in our opinion, the current cabinet has completed its mission and is on the path of retreat.

US Major General Proposes Establishing a Ministry of National Defense 265

Says a Pacific War is Hard to Avoid

Should Urgently Complete the Five-Year Air Force Plan

Tokyo Nichinichi Shimbun, April 1st, says that former US Army Air Force Commander Major General William Mitchell, on the 30th of last month, submitted a proposal to the House of Representatives' Army Committee, arguing that the US Army and Navy should be controlled by one leader and a new Ministry of National Defense should be established in order to enhance the performance of US military strength and reduce national defense expenditures. He said that a Pacific war is practically unavoidable. If we want to realize the enhancement of the efficiency of the national army and save more than 250 million national defense expenditures annually, the national defense organization should be implemented immediately. The method is to first place the three armies of the army, navy, and air force under the jurisdiction of one leader and establish a new Ministry of National Defense, and the main national defense issues of the United States should be concentrated in the Pacific, because on the Pacific coast there is a strong and powerful country in the world competing for hegemony, and that country actually holds the ambition of Genghis Khan's expedition, so it will soon conflict with us. Under these circumstances, it would be a great mistake for the United States not to strengthen its air force.

In addition, the Hochi Shimbun reported that US Army Aviation Commander Major General Flourice explained the essentials of the US national defense system at the Army Committee on March 31, arguing that the construction of battleships should be suspended in order to strengthen the air force. His review of the US armed forces was originally an important political program of the Democratic Party during its time in opposition. Now, the United States should urgently change its national defense system and study appropriate measures. All battleships should be stopped immediately. The future policy of the United States is limited to not invading foreign territory. In future naval battles, it is usually within the range of the flight of a base on land. This is what I have learned from my research on the history of naval warfare over the past 300 years. In the past, the emphasis was on defending the inland, but now the strength of the US Air Force is only enough to defend half of the country. Since 1926, the five-year continuous project of strengthening the air force has been approved by Congress. It has been seven years now, but this plan has not yet been completed due to saving expenses. According to the five-year plan, the US Air Force should have 1,800 army aircraft, but the actual strength now is less than 285. If the necessary aircraft that are indispensable to national defense are further reduced in size by saving expenses, how can the safety of the country be guaranteed?

Anglo-American Conflict and the War Debt Problem (London Correspondence) (March 3) 276

British Chamberlain, in his speech in Leith, stated that at the end of last year, the United States initiated a debt conference. Britain has not yet formally expressed its acceptance of this conference. However, when the meeting is held in the future, it will first put forward two demands: complete and permanent cancellation of war debts and recognition of the Lausanne Treaty by the United States. Regarding this issue, American newspapers have strongly opposed it. The "New York American," under Hearst's trust, made a severe critique in a commentary, being the most intense among the opposing voices. The commentary stated, "Chamberlain's words are simply a disgrace to Britain. Such words should be treated like foolish talk and simply ignored." A certain member of the House of Lords even suggested arresting Baruch, who was commissioned by Roosevelt to negotiate a partial cancellation of war debts with Britain and France, proposing to reduce war debts by 75 percent.

Although the Lausanne Treaty ostensibly "reduced" German reparations to 300 million marks, the treaty also had another provision that the final implementation of the treaty was conditional on the United States abandoning war debts. The most recent payment of war debts due from France to the United States has not yet been paid. Herriot even fell from power because he advocated paying the debt. After the exchange of notes between Britain and the United States in the past period, Britain repaid the December debt, but at the same time declared that this repayment was the last repayment.

The United States feels the danger that debtor countries have formed a united front, with all debtor countries using the excuse that their payment of debts must be contingent on Germany's payment of reparations as the main reason. They also demand that the United States reduce or cancel the war debts owed to it in proportion to the "reduction" of German reparations under the Lausanne Treaty. The United States strongly believes that Germany's payment of reparations has nothing to do with the repayment of American war debts, and argues that the payment of war debts should be based on the principle of ability to pay. In reality, the United States has indeed broken up the | | slowly formed | | united front formed by debtor countries. Britain,

The United Kingdom and Italy have re-acknowledged payment after Hoover issued a moratorium. The United States invites these debtor countries to make individual debt negotiations, giving them the opportunity to partially reduce their debts, as a "reward" for acknowledging payment. There has been no invitation to negotiate with France, which is "defaulting," and Poland, which has not paid its debts on time.

The United States has fortunately broken up the united front of debtor countries, but fierce disputes have arisen in negotiations between the United States and Britain. We have already briefly shown some of these disputes in the press above. For the United States, this is not just a matter of the amount of war debt, although this total is always considerable, amounting to hundreds of millions of dollars. The demands of the United States go far beyond this. Currently, Britain, France, and Japan have virtually formed an alliance in the Far East, while the efforts of American foreign policy are precisely in the Far East. Due to its isolation, it is greatly threatened by Japanese actions. Therefore, the United States is extremely willing to use this as a powerful tool for its foreign policy. In addition, the United States has also indicated that it is willing to base the reduction or cancellation of debts on an exchange of British political and economic conditions.

The United States believes that these possible other conditions for exchange are, first, the restoration of the gold standard by Britain; second, preferential tariffs for American products in the British Empire market; third, concessions on the issue of armaments; and fourth, diplomatic assistance from Britain exerting political pressure on other debtors of the United States by virtue of British claims or British investment.

The current Anglo-American conflict, due to disagreements on the war debt issue, is almost blatantly exposed. If Britain does not express obedience, the United States will not hesitate to threaten Britain. As a result, British and Commonwealth imports to the United States will continue to be greatly restricted. The United States has already instigated its protectorates to wage war against British forces in South America, and further intensification of American anti-British forces in South America is expected.

Britain is also unwilling to concede and is urgently seeking appropriate countermeasures. In fact, Japan's policy of plundering China can provide Britain with ample assistance. Even Chamberlain's speech in Leith mentioned that, to the extent possible, Britain must increase its exports to the United States or reduce American imports to Britain. Although Chamberlain immediately stated that this was by no means a threat, the American government and public opinion have not changed their opinion of Chamberlain's speech because of this.

The global economic panic, like Germany's payment of reparations, has made it impossible for countries to pay American war debts. The general disastrous fall in prices has increased the responsibility of payment, and the large financial deficits of all debtor countries have made raising funds completely impossible. Even if the debt could be raised, the exchange rate issue would still become an unavoidable obstacle, because there are tariff barriers everywhere, making it impossible to raise the necessary amount. This difficulty is further exacerbated by the United States' withdrawal of its large daily investments abroad. If the United States could implement the heavy artillery to deal with all debtor countries and force them to pay their debts, then the Lausanne Treaty would naturally be cancelled automatically. That is to say, the cancellation of the Young Plan is conditional on the implementation of the Lausanne Treaty. Now that the Lausanne Treaty is invalid, the Young Plan is back in effect.

From this, it can be seen that the entire imperialist conflict, due to the intensification of the Anglo-American war debt issue, has reached a very high degree. Moreover, this conflict is a conflict between two pivotal powers and the main battle line of the struggle between the two powers.

Severe Drought Across Shaanxi Province 277

Sounds of selling wives and children heard everywhere

The strong beg while the weak starve to death

Xi'an Correspondence: The drought in various parts of Shaanxi Province is extremely severe. The investigation is as follows:

People and Animals Eating Each Other in Xianyang 278

Xu Jiheng, chairman of the Xianyang Relief Association, yesterday submitted a report to the Provincial Relief Association stating that since the beginning of this spring, there has been no rain, and the drought has become more severe. Wheat seedlings and weeds have all withered. In this critical moment for the people, when life and death are hopeless, they want to sell their wives and children to get food, but their wives and children have long been sold. They want to demolish houses and destroy farm tools to make a living, but their houses and tools have long been exhausted. Looking ahead, there is deep fear. At this time of disaster after disaster, when nine out of ten lives are lost, some commit suicide by hanging or poisoning, some abandon their children in wells and flee alone, and some parents starve to death together. Now, death is everywhere, dogs and pigs are fighting for food, and flies and maggots are swarming. Therefore, when entering the territory, there are no traces of human habitation, and withering is everywhere. Even if there are surviving remnants, people are thin and emaciated, living in thatched huts and broken windows, eating tree bark and grass roots. Since the disaster, there has never been such a tragic and severe situation. What did the people of Xianyang do to deserve this great calamity? If no measures are taken to provide relief, I fear that the people of Xianyang will cease to be people, and the county will cease to be a county. Please allocate funds for relief to save lives.

A Thousand Starved to Death in Fuping 279

This spring in Fuping, there was a lack of rain, wheat seedlings withered, and drought was widespread. The area of the second district is even more barren and bitter. Therefore, people fleeing to other places are endless. Those who have not fled rely entirely on digging up wheat vegetable roots to survive. Demolishing and selling houses and fields is common, and some even sell their wives and children. Now, the vegetable roots and tree bark have been almost completely dug up, and clothes and property have long been exhausted. Their hardship has reached the extreme, crying for food. How can they survive? According to the current survey, more than half of the households in the entire district have fled, and the disaster situation has become more urgent recently. In two months, more than a thousand people have fled or starved to death, and there are as many as three thousand unemployed. Now, only one-tenth of the livestock remains, and there are more than four thousand acres of wasteland. Even if it rains, there will be no way to plant.

Father and Son Weeping Together in Chengcheng 280

The county is barren and the people are poor, and there are no rich households or big merchants. The residents all make a living by farming. Since the seventeenth year of the Republic, there has been a severe drought every year, and harvests have been poor every year. The people's savings are repeatedly exhausted, and villages have become ruins. Last autumn, there was no harvest again, and this spring, it is not raining, the wheat seedlings are withered and yellow, and there is no hope for the summer harvest. Selling wives and children is common, and suicides by poisoning occur frequently. Orphans and widows wander along the roads, the benevolent pot is broken, and fathers and sons weep together. All these tragic scenes are difficult to describe in detail. Therefore, the county deeply hopes that benevolent people will distribute rice and grain as soon as possible to save these survivors.

Seven Dead in Baishui 281

Since the 17th year of the Republic of China, Baishui has experienced drought for five years, and the people have been displaced. It is painful to talk about it, and the southeast corner is particularly severe. Last year, not a single grain of wheat was harvested in the autumn. During the winter, people took their elderly and children to escape to the northern mountains because they had no food. Those who remained in their homes were all disabled. To this day, seven or eight out of ten have starved to death. Currently, the sky is still dry, and although there are wheat seedlings, they are all withered and also infested with insects. Therefore, even those who have not died have been eaten. From last October to the present, the turnips have been completely dug up and eaten. Now, all the family property has been sold, and there is nothing to do but wait for death. If relief is not provided quickly, I fear that these disaster victims will also perish.

Not a Blade of Grass Grows in Linzhou 282

Since the beginning of spring in Linzhou, there has been no rain, and the land is barren for thousands of miles, and not a blade of grass grows. Now, grains are rarely seen in the market. Wealthy families initially survived on wheat bran, oil residue, vinegar dregs, and wild vegetables. Recently, wheat bran has also become scarce, so oil residue is considered the best. When trying to peel tree bark, there is no bark to peel. When trying to dig up vegetable roots, there is nothing to dig up. Even buckwheat flowers, chaff, and peach bark cost hundreds of dollars per liter. Some have even buried their children alive because they have no way to survive, and some have committed suicide. Those who die from tiger epidemics are also everywhere. In total, the entire county, excluding those who have been burned or infected by bandits or died of hunger, has fewer than 1,500 households of widowers, widows, orphans, and young women and children. Their faces are thin and emaciated, and the sounds of crying for hunger and cold are constantly heard, making the situation extremely distressing.

Disaster Victims Leaving the Pass to Beg for Food 283

Disaster victims in Tongguan are gathering and unable to go east. The county magistrate of the county previously drafted measures for leaving the border and submitted them to the provincial government for transfer to the railway bureau for transportation. However, due to the sudden cold weather, more and more disaster victims are gathering. The county magistrate and various agencies fear that accidents will occur, so they raised funds to hire ships to temporarily send the disaster victims east. Yesterday, they also sent a telegram to the provincial government for review. The telegram stated, "The county magistrate is responsible for submitting a telegram on cold days, along with proposed measures for transporting disaster victims leaving the border, respectfully requesting review and instructions, and requesting a telegram to Henan Province to allow disaster victims to enter and pass through the province, and a telegram to the Ministry of Railways to notify the railway bureau to allow them to travel by train. However, the review and transfer telegram will take time, and the number of disaster victims passing through the border is increasing. Moreover, due to the recent strong winds and sudden cold weather, it is impossible to wait, and the demand for transportation is becoming more urgent. The county magistrate and various agencies fear that delays will cause accidents. They decided at a meeting today to have the garrison and local agencies and charities take care of the disaster victims, temporarily sending them by boat to the Shaanxi Prefecture and Lingbao Xiang areas to disembark, so that they can find ways to go east again. They will also conduct inspections during boarding and distribute food appropriately. The cost of this food will be raised by various agencies, merchants, and others. Once the previously submitted measures are reviewed, they will be transported by train. The county government of Guan County and various agencies respectfully request approval (April 3rd)."

Four Provinces Discussing the Aftermath of the Yao Rebellion 284

Treat Everyone Equally by Cutting Hair and Changing Clothes

Do Not Differentiate Between Yao and Miao People, Allow Them to Live Together

Changsha Correspondence: The border areas of Hunan, Guangxi, Yunnan, and Guizhou provinces have always been places where Yao and Miao people gather. Last month, Yao people in Xing'an, Quanyang, Longsheng, and other counties in Guangxi Province were incited by communists to advocate that the Yao King had descended from heaven to revive the Yao and destroy the Han, gathering tens of thousands of people to launch a major riot, which extended to Hunan Province. Yao people in more than a dozen counties in the border areas of Hunan and Guangxi provinces rose up in response, and the situation escalated. Fortunately, the Yao and Miao people did not have many guns and weapons, and the Hunan and Guangxi provinces dealt with them quickly. The Yao King was also captured by the Yongming County team in Hunan, and the remaining crowds fled into the Yao Mountains. However, although the Yao rebellion has temporarily been quelled, if the soothing and aftermath work is not handled properly, there could be future troubles. Huang Xuchu, chairman of Guangxi Province, focused on organizing baojia, making the Yao people cut their hair and change their clothes, treating them equally with the Han people, and abolishing the names of Yao and Miao people in order to fundamentally eliminate the Yao rebellion. In addition to ordering the counties in Guangxi to comply, he also telegraphed Hunan, Yunnan, Guizhou, and other provinces, requesting that they handle it consistently to curb the source of the chaos. Chairman He of Hunan Province greatly approved of this and also advocated further planning for the Yao people's livelihoods, stabilizing their lives, developing education, fundamentally eliminating boundaries, and implementing co-residence with the Han people. The exchange of telegrams between the two sides is as follows: (1) Telegram from Chairman Huang of Guangxi: "To Chairman He Yunqiao of Changsha, Chairman Wang Shaowu of Guiyang, and Chairman Long Zhidan of Yunnan: I have investigated that the Yao people in Xing'an, Quanyang, Guangyin, Longsheng, and other counties in my province were secretly incited by communists, first by building altars and offering sacrifices to gods to incite the Yao people, and then by advocating that the Yao King had descended from heaven to revive the Yao and destroy the Han, raising flags and gathering crowds, and rushing out in separate ways to attack Xing'an and Quanyang counties. For a time, the counties adjacent to each other had many followers, and the situation escalated. My brother and Jian Gong (Bai Chongxi) learned from the handling of the Wuyuan Yao case in Guanyang last year that we should focus on soothing and not punish them in any way. Learning from the past, we will start with a painful suppression to deal with this situation, so that they will suffer a heavy blow. Then we will talk about soothing, so that we can promote their awakening and repentance, fear our power, and embrace our virtue, and dare not rebel again. We have ordered the army and militia to cooperate in suppressing them. According to telegrams, the Yao bandits in each county have been swept away by the army and militia. A small number of them have fled to the border areas of Hunan and Guizhou, and the rest have been gradually eliminated. We are now handling the aftermath and have strictly ordered the punishment of the leaders and the dissolution of those who were coerced. At the same time, we are organizing villages and jia, making the Yao people cut their hair and change their clothes, treating them equally with the Han people, and abolishing the names of Miao and Yao people in order to eliminate boundaries. This is the general situation of my province's handling of the Yao rebellion. However, according to reports, the Communist Party's contact with the Yao people in Hunan, Yunnan, Guizhou, and other provinces seems to have political implications and cannot be ignored. Although my province has handled it quickly and come to a conclusion, your province has many Yao tribes mixed together, and the Yao Mountains are dangerous. It is inevitable that there will be communists lurking, secretly bewitching people, and acting rashly upon hearing the news. Please investigate and order your subordinates to pay attention and handle it consistently to curb the source of the chaos and jointly maintain border security. Please reply. Your brother Huang Xuchu kowtows. (2) Reply telegram from He Jian: "To Chairman Huang Xuchu of Nanning: I have received your telegram with respect. The Yao bandits in Xing'an and Guan in your province have become a riot and have become an expanded force. My brother and Jian Gong have commanded with certainty and quickly put down the riot. You have also ordered the organization of baojia, cutting hair and changing clothes, and treating them equally with the Han people, which shows your awe-inspiring power and your ability to soothe and govern from afar. I greatly admire you and will comply and handle it consistently to curb the source of the chaos. However, I intend to make proper plans for their livelihoods to stabilize them, revitalize education, and transform their ignorance. Border security is of utmost importance. Please give me temporary instructions. Your brother He Jian kowtows." He also sent telegrams to the authorities in Guizhou and Yunnan, requesting that they handle it consistently in this way. A Fraudster Who Combined Deception and Robbery 302

Fortunately Discovered by Yang Xichen

Wei Fugen Sentenced to 30 Days of Detention

Wei Fugen, from Wuxi, yesterday at 11:30 AM on Tiantong Road, colluded with a rogue child named A Qi to impersonate a genuine ring and fraudulently sell a copper counterfeit ring to pedestrians. Just then, Wang Fuzhen, a peasant from Chongming, arrived carrying a cotton quilt, staggering along. Wei immediately instructed the child to peddle the ring to Wang, saying that if he wanted to get rich, he could buy this cheap item, that this ring was worth dozens of yuan but was now being sold for only one yuan. Wang Fuzhen, having just arrived in Shanghai from the countryside, was unaware of the scam and could not recognize the counterfeit. His heart was moved, and he took out a Yuan head coin (silver dollar) from his pocket to buy it. Seeing Wang fall for the trap, Wei approached the child and falsely claimed that he was willing to offer four yuan for the ring, implying that there was a large profit to be made. The child, understanding the signal, demanded the original item back from Wang, who refused. The child then demanded an additional three yuan. As Wang had no more money, Wei mediated, suggesting that Wang pawn his cotton quilt at Hengxing Pawnshop at No. 168 on the road for three yuan to compensate the child. Wang Fuzhen was confused by the gang's tricks, and Wei forcibly pawned the quilt on his behalf, handing him the pawn ticket. As they were whispering in front of the pawnshop, Yang Xichen, a Chinese detective from the Hongkou Precinct, passed by and noticed their suspicious behavior. After questioning them, he realized that Wang had been deceived. He immediately arrested Wei, while the child escaped in the meantime. Both the counterfeit ring, the pawn ticket, and the silver coin were taken to the police station. This morning, they were escorted to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District. Zhang Tianyin, the police lawyer, explained the situation, presenting the counterfeit ring for inspection. The victim, Wang Fuzhen, stated that he had come from his hometown in search of his brother but was cheated by the defendant. When questioned, Wei Fugen's statements were evasive. Judge Wu Zehan sentenced Wei to thirty days of detention as a warning, and the quilt was returned to the original owner.

Talking Points

The Enthralled by Officialdom Mr. Liang, the God of Wealth 303

— Li

Mr. Liang Zuoyou, who caused a sensation worldwide with the fictitious claim of uncovering the wealth of thirty million from the son of Jie Yuan, earning the title of "Living God of Wealth," suddenly disappeared from public attention for half a year. It turns out the old gentleman was writing behind closed doors and has completed a magnificent work, the "National Thrift and Salvation Plan." Unfortunately, we do not have the good fortune of Chairman Han and Secretary-General Zhang to have a sneak peek at the whole picture!

According to reports, this "National Thrift and Salvation Plan" is roughly divided into "establishing a National Thrift and Salvation Committee, democratically elected members, establishing a National Thrift and Salvation Bank, issuing two hundred million yuan in Salvation Currency." The phrase "National Salvation" appears in every other sentence, proving that Mr. Liang is ultimately a "God of Wealth Enthusiastic About National Salvation," capable of writing such a "three sentences inseparable from action" "National Salvation Plan." Mr. Liang previously boasted in Beijing that "the lost territory of the Northeast can be recovered in one hundred and eight days," so the value of this plan must be equal to the Heavenly Book without Words of the Nine Heavens Mysterious Lady, needless to say. It is no wonder that those who obtain it keep it secret and do not disclose it.

However, is Mr. Liang truly a Zhang Jiao and Zhang Bao, or a person afflicted with mental illness? Certainly not. Listening to his crazy and absurd talk, it seems like he is suffering from severe mental illness, but carefully considering his inner psychology, he is actually extremely "enthralled by officialdom," but unable to achieve it, and thus repeatedly resorts to fantasy, hoping to cleverly take advantage of luck!

Why do I say this? The method for raising funds for the National Salvation Bank in the plan is that each of the four hundred million people in the country has a piggy bank, contributing one copper coin per day, with a two-year term, paying two yuan per term. After ten years, two hundred million yuan can be raised to complete the National Salvation Plan and National Salvation work. Whether this is so easy or not is beside the point, but the five installments of payments would require a total of two hundred million piggy banks. How can they be manufactured in time? And how to account for such a huge expense for piggy banks? Therefore, with such a "National Salvation Plan" of deceiving oneself as well as others, Mr. Liang also clearly knows that it is difficult to achieve practical results, but the intention of the drunkard is not in the wine, but in wanting to be elected as a member of the "National Thrift and Salvation Committee," which must be established first, or the president and other important positions of the "National Thrift and Salvation Bank"!

Let us further examine the use of the two hundred million yuan in currency issued in his plan. Twenty percent is for military expenses for "suppressing the communists" and "resisting foreign invasion," and for "disaster relief," while sixty percent is for "developing industries." The remaining twenty percent, amounting to four hundred million yuan, does not specify its intended use. It is likely that "the wool comes from the sheep," and it is pre-planned by Mr. Liang as the expenses for the two major institutions, the "National Thrift and Salvation Committee" and the "National Thrift and Salvation Bank," or as the cost of purchasing two hundred million piggy banks. If this is really the case, then Mr. Liang, the God of Wealth, clearly possesses the basic skills to become a high-ranking official. From now on, with added effort, it is not difficult to transform from a commoner into a powerful and influential official!

However, those who "hang a sheep's head and sell dog meat," using the banner of reforming society to create a special territory, and using the name of jointly facing national difficulties to hunt for their own positions and wealth, are there only Liang, the God of Wealth, who is "enthralled by officialdom" in the vast land of China?

Science

Oxyhydrogen Blowpipe 304

— Gong Weiyu

In large ironworks, we often see them use a device with an iron pipe at the front and two rubber tubes connected at the back. The iron pipe emits countless sparks and flames, and when sprayed onto any ironware, it quickly melts or pierces it. How amazing! This is what I want to talk about:

Oxyhydrogen Blowpipe. Before I explain it, I need to describe the combustion process of hydrogen and oxygen:

(1) Hydrogen is a spontaneous combustible substance. It ignites upon contact with fire, and although its flame is weak, its temperature is extremely high.

(2) Oxygen is a combustion-supporting substance. Even a small spark can ignite instantly when it encounters sufficient oxygen. If a large amount of oxygen is supplied during combustion, the temperature can reach over two thousand degrees Celsius.

These two gases can be separately stored in sturdy cylindrical iron containers under extremely high pressure to supply the oxyhydrogen blowpipe.

Now, let's talk about the oxyhydrogen blowpipe itself.

The oxyhydrogen blowpipe is made of steel, but the nozzle that emits the flame is made of a heat-resistant alloy. The front is pipe-shaped, and the back is box-shaped, with a tube connected to the rubber tube attached to the hydrogen cylinder. Another tube is connected to the oxygen cylinder via the box-shaped part and leads to the flame nozzle. Because it connects to the flame nozzle, it does not mix with hydrogen before being sprayed out. If hydrogen and oxygen mix and burn beforehand, it will explode, causing loud noises and other dangers! Each tube for hydrogen or oxygen has a valve that can be opened and closed freely.

When in use, simply open the valves. Hydrogen and oxygen are compressed in the cylinders, so when they find an outlet, they quickly escape through the rubber tubes and are separately sprayed out from the nozzle. When the hydrogen is ignited, it burns, and because a large amount of oxygen is supplied, an extremely intense flame is emitted. The temperature is so high that it can melt all kinds of strong and difficult-to-melt metals. It is very quick to use an oxyhydrogen blowpipe to cut steel plates and pierce thick steel plates.

But unfortunately, oxyhydrogen blowpipes and all accessories come from foreign countries. I hope our country can also imitate them to fill the gaps.

A Small Boat Heavily Laden with Distant Hopes

Talking About Aviation Saving the Nation 305

— Xihe Master

The call for aviation to save the nation has been growing louder. Rumors of compromises are swirling, and the storm is gathering. In this critical autumn, we should rely on facts and take the power of the people as a premise. We should not allow people to have doubts and hesitations. Recently, the matter of using aviation to save the nation has been responded to almost throughout the country. Taking Shanghai as an example, businesses, schools, and organizations are all rising up like a storm. However, examining the results, there is a real lack of energy. The busy district and diverse city should have responded to the call, but the results for the past month have not reached even one or two percent. Is it because there is no one to lead the effort, or because the system is not specialized? Things have their own advantages, gathering every bit to make a fur coat, and accumulating sand to form a tower. This is known and believed by everyone, but even many rhinos cannot withstand repeated skinning, and the end of a strong crossbow cannot pierce Lu silk. Comparing Peng Zu and Shang Zi in terms of lifespan, and equating Lou Li with wealth, the rich are just one hair of nine oxen, while the poor are exhausting their resources to search for every last bit. How many people are not trying to avoid and hide? Why do I say that? Let me provide evidence to support my words.

The Aviation Association is responsible for the overall matter, and the Shanghai School of the Education Association promotes its success. There are also local community organizations and institutions. A friend of mine has a family of eight, with two sons and four daughters. Except for the two youngest, who are still in swaddling clothes, the rest are studying at a certain Cantonese school in Shanghai. My friend earns thirty yuan a month. Apart from food, clothing, and housing, the education expenses of his children have become a stretch. Last night, in the rain, he came to borrow money, saying it was urgent for saving the nation. I said, "How strange! You are like Weisheng Gao!" My friend then told me about the donation. As he is a teacher, middle school teachers are required to join the Aviation Association as members, and the Shanghai School aircraft also has the obligation to donate. As he is from Guangdong, the Guangdong aircraft cannot be an exception, and his children also have the so-called minimum donation. At the time, he listed a detailed account as follows:

Family Budget for April

Income: Thirty yuan a month. Expenses: Rent eight yuan, food sixteen yuan, spring school uniform six yuan, Aviation Association membership fee (self two yuan, four children four yuan) totaling six yuan, Shanghai School aircraft donation (self two yuan, two children two yuan and four jiao (tenths of a yuan) and a half) totaling four yuan and six jiao and a half, Children's Army aircraft / Guangdong aircraft, amount undetermined.

According to the above table, my friend will have a significant overdraft this month. My friend said to me, "Save the nation, or save myself? I cannot have both. Which should I prioritize?" I said, "National affairs are public affairs, and personal affairs are private affairs. You are in education and should understand the distinction between the small self and the big self. How can you harm the public for personal gain? You came to my door to borrow money for saving the nation, which is reasonable. I will use my surplus resources to help you in your emergency, which is righteous. However, my situation is the same as yours. I will also borrow from others for this matter. What can I do? Why don't you go home and think of another plan?" My friend remained silent for a long time and returned dejectedly. I also thought with concern, lamenting that it is impossible to be a citizen in a declining world.

The Three Satisfactions of the Japanese 306

— Boming

The Japanese regard the three northeastern provinces as Manchuria. With tens of thousands of troops, they occupied Manchuria in less than three months, and the whole country is proud and arrogant, one can say they are smug. They also hold Fu Yi and Fu Wei, two or three Manchus, and implement the old tricks of annihilating Korea in the independence of Manchuria. From the above, the Japanese are satisfied, holding Manchus, and occupying Manchuria. The first satisfaction is without dissatisfaction. The book says that satisfaction invites loss, and the Jin people's inscription says that satisfaction leads to collapse. The moon also wanes when it is full, and excessive population becomes a problem. The word satisfaction is extremely ominous, and the Japanese are satisfied, holding Manchus, and occupying Manchuria. How can they not be harmed, collapse, wane, and become a problem?

Geneva Crumbles

Since the September 18th Incident last year, our country has relied on the League of Nations for everything. The League of Nations is located in Geneva. Recently, the Japanese have invaded Rehe, and the League of Nations is still unable to find fault. Recently, the Japanese blatantly withdrew from the League of Nations, causing us to be consistently disappointed in the League of Nations, and the country itself is quite dangerous. Those who say that Japan in Geneva means that the League of Nations in Geneva will crumble. According to recent reports, Japan's domestic economy is increasingly panicked because of the "Manchukuo" situation of wanting to maintain the illegitimate son of Japan. Geneva means that the Japanese internal will crumble.

Saving the Nation with Imported Goods! 307

— Leyi

I live in a south-facing room that is spacious, bright, and conveniently located on the dormitory's thoroughfare. My roommates are wealthy students who have endless boxes of snacks and are good at socializing, so many students leave their rooms and sit in ours all day, except when they have classes.

School has started, and our room has become a reception room again. The floor is covered with wrappers from foreign candies and fruit peels. Newspapers with movie advertisements and magazines with nude pictures are scattered on the tables and beds. Sometimes, there are also the smells of cigarettes and coffee, which are strictly prohibited by the school, lingering in our room.

In the first few days of school, there isn't much heavy homework, so our room becomes even more lively, but their conversations are mostly repetitive.

"What did you do for fun during the winter vacation?"

"Nothing but watching movies."

"Did you watch them every day? What did you watch?"

"At least once a day, and sometimes two or three times. I only watch imported movies because Chinese movies lack passion and sensuality compared to foreign movies. They can't arouse my interest. And foreign movies aren't expensive, only one or two yuan."

"Wow, young master! Young master!" The speaker pretends to be both mocking and envious.

"Huh! One or two yuan is nothing. Look at the style of my leather shoes. They're imported and cost more than twenty-six yuan!" A person wearing shiny leather shoes walks back and forth a few steps, saying with pride.

"Humph, what's so special about leather shoes? Look at my suit. It was custom-made at a foreign store for more than a hundred yuan in labor and materials," another person straightens out their brand-new suit, saying even more proudly.

Then watches, pens, gloves, silk stockings, and so on are taken out of everyone's pockets and boxes, and they all say they are imported goods.

Not only in our room, but also in other places, I often hear these kinds of conversations.

"Ah! Saving the nation with imported goods!" This is the thought that comes to me after hearing these conversations.

Young people, we, the young people of this national crisis, should shoulder the task of saving the nation, strive to reach the highest point in our physical, moral, and intellectual development, and use domestic goods.

Now, let's see what our work of saving the nation is: looking at imported goods, wearing imported goods, using imported goods, and eating imported goods.

"Ah! Isn't this saving the nation with imported goods!" I thought.

Third-Class Ward 308

— Hong

Living in this realistic society where economics take precedence, the poor are least able to fall ill. Otherwise, they only have one option: to sit and await death. Naturally, it's not a certainty that once the illness strikes, their life is forfeit, but ultimately, misfortune outweighs fortune. Recently, P fell ill. Although he was a poor scholar, the illness he contracted was a so-called "rich man's disease." He had a high tumor on his neck, terribly red and swollen, requiring surgery to be effective. So, how to pay for this large medical expense became the problem. In the end, he had no choice but to go to the XXXXX branch hospital, established for charity and to care for the common people.

A corner of the third-class ward of the XXXXX branch hospital:

"Thank you, could you change it to some watery porridge? " A weak, trembling voice called out, requesting the female nurse not far from the bed to help him change the porridge. "..." She only gave him a cunning glance, deliberately remaining silent.

"Um, please change it to some watery porridge, can you hear me?"

"What's wrong? Why do you want that kind of porridge? Always complaining!"

"Yes, I want some cleaner porridge. This bowl is mixed with dust and has a bit of a muttony smell. I'm afraid it's not hygienic."

"How strange, you have the nerve to say that. Getting this yellow millet porridge in the third-class ward is already generous enough. Heh, cleaner? Go to the first or second-class ward! Then!"

"Please forgive a poor patient like us, please be lenient! Thank you, please don't keep grumbling!"

"Bah! How much are you paying the hospital? Not to mention the food and lodging. We provide it to you openly. If you don't want to follow the rules here, you can leave the hospital immediately." She said threateningly, "Not long ago, there was another patient just like you, who was kicked out of the hospital by the director. You better watch yourself."

"Nurse, nurse, please come." After P accepted her lecture, she turned away coquettishly. P, still with his humble attitude, hoped for a last glimmer of hope: "Never mind, never mind. But now my head feels very heavy, I have a headache, and pus is flowing from the tumor, please treat it quickly."

"How ridiculous, nurse, nurse? What bad luck."

"Miss Zhang, please forgive me, I was wrong." Pitiful P, while groaning in pain, apologized to her. He quickly remembered what K in the same ward had said: Don't yell at the nurses, call them "Miss" and "小姐," that might be more appropriate....

"Humph, you want me to apologize and flatter you? We are not nurses to be bossed around at will. We are just here for internship from the nursing class. Who wants to be bothered with you people?"

Time flies like smoke, and now it's midnight again. P was in too much pain to sleep. He sadly thought again about the lecture he received for the "porridge" and the "pus flowing from the tumor." He thought silently: This hospital is supposed to be for charity and to care for the common people, how can there be such strange phenomena? Although she is here for an internship, if she learns this kind of skill to deceive the common people during her internship, and later rises to the position of a doctor, alas, I don't know how many lives she will ruin? A burst of teasing laughter came from behind the curtain across the window, and he vaguely saw her and the fat Doctor Huang embracing and kissing passionately. He then deliberately dragged his voice and yawned:

"Damn, what 'Miss', '小姐'? They don't even turn off the lights, daring to play such a trick in front of so many patients, it's truly outrageous!"

"What's the matter? What's the matter?"

"Shhh..."

Clerk Correspondence

Working for Others for Free 309

Editor:

My three-year apprenticeship has passed (now in the fourth year); but I have not yet received any salary from the business owner, as a sign that he treats me as an employee. I work hard all day long, will there never be any compensation? How disappointing! Because my family is under heavy economic pressure, and still relies on my strength to help them out!

Now I want to ask the business owner to give me a salary; but the cunning business owner, seeing that I often have a dissatisfied attitude, has already made it clear: He says, "It's hard to find a job now, there are people who are willing to work for others for free, without any compensation, just to get a bite to eat, but we don't even want them!" Indeed, it is difficult to find a place to eat now, and he uses this point to make people afraid to complain under his exploitation. So, he usually doesn't allow people to read newspapers or do academic research, perhaps to make people ignorant and let him exploit them! Editor, if this continues, what should I do? I am not that young anymore.

The only solution is to find another job. But I have limited talent and knowledge, what can I do happily and competently? Moreover, I have no connections, and no high school or university qualifications, it's really difficult! Your newspaper's amateur weekly's "Self-Job Introduction" is indeed a life-saving ring for the general public who have no prominent relatives and want to find a job. However, judging from this letter, I don't know if I can do anything else? I also don't know if people like me are allowed to publish it? Please, wise editor, give me an instruction. You are solving difficulties for many people, I eagerly await your reply! Sincerely, Cai Jidong

乂　　　乂　　　乂　　乂

Editor's Note: In this recession year, everyone is talking about "tightening" and "unemployment." There are indeed many people who only want to eat a meal and don't expect to be paid. But capitalists should not take advantage of this opportunity to exploit the poor. You should make full use of your powerful capital to develop your business and accommodate these many unemployed people. We don't dare to sing high-pitched songs and tell you to give away your wealth; but you should know that reducing one unemployed person today is removing a dangerous element from society. They are indeed directly benefiting, but you can also indirectly obtain security. What's not to like about this kind of win-win situation? If you are short-sighted, only know the immediate benefits, disregard the suffering of others, and exploit them blindly, then once it breaks down, the society will be in chaos, and "if the skin is gone, what will the hair cling to?"

Judging from Cai Jun's letter (without any changes), the writing is clear and coherent, and the thinking is correct. With your talent, it is not very difficult to find a job. It's strange to say, when everywhere is full of unemployed people, there are many places that are playing the trick of "not using good people"! Cai Jun, you don't need to worry too much, because besides the place you are working now, there are many places in the world that need people!

Novel

Time in a Dream (Continued 23) 310

— Qin Shouou

Ju Fen was huddled in a pile of embroidered quilts, her face as haggard as a flower lacking rain and dew. Her two crescent-shaped eyebrows were tightly furrowed. She gave Wu Yi an unnatural smile when she saw him.

"It... hurts a lot here..." She pointed to her throat with her slender fingers.

"A sore throat? How bad is it?" Wu Yi was almost standing on the edge of her bed.

She nodded slowly.

"Have you seen a doctor?" Wu Yi bent down halfway, the two faces less than a foot apart. Ju Fen slowly shook her left hand, but covered her mouth with her right hand, as if afraid of infecting Wu Yi with her throat ailment.

"I'll call for you!" Wu Yi turned around and left, meaning to go downstairs to call for a doctor for Ju Fen.

"Don't go! Don't go! I'm afraid..." Ju Fen stubbornly objected, because she had suffered enough pain from an illness after giving birth, and she became afraid when people mentioned doctors.

Wu Yi knew that she was very stubborn, so he stopped obediently and thought silently.

"Ah! I'll go buy some medicine for you!" Immediately, he thought of the special medicines for throat ailments, "Hydrogen Peroxide Water" and "Formamint Lozenges." Without asking for Ju Fen's consent, he ran downstairs like a wisp of smoke.

The XXXXX Village area had few shops because it was a residential area. There were practically no pharmacies, but there was a car rental company. Wu Yi quickly hired a car and rushed to Nanjing Road as if he were robbing it. He bought a bottle of medicine pills and two bottles of medicine water, and specially brought two yuan's worth of Florida oranges, which Ju Fen loved to eat. He returned in the same hired car.

This was almost the end of the month. Usually, Wu Yi spent money very freely. His wife limited his allowance of sixty yuan, and by the 24th or 25th, it was often used up. Today, he only had eight yuan left in his pocket; the car fare, medicine, and oranges, coincidentally, were exactly used up.

Because he had emptied his pockets, Wu Yi couldn't afford to hire a car as usual when he returned home at half past ten that night. He had no choice but to walk home, and was covered in sweat by the time he arrived. Unexpectedly, this small secret was seen through by the clever and quick-witted Sister A Jin, who reported it to Ju Fen word for word.

"Please take this letter and read it!" The next day, Wu Yi went to the Wang family an hour earlier. According to Ju Fen, the sore throat had been relieved a lot, and he was naturally extremely happy. When he was about to leave, Ju Fen suddenly took out a light yellow envelope from under the pillow she was leaning on and handed it to Wu Yi, but she didn't allow him to open it immediately, asking him to open and read it after he left the door.

As soon as he stepped out of the door, Wu Yi couldn't help but open this mysterious envelope. Inside, there were two ten-yuan bills and a sheet of women's pink paper. There were a few very cursive pencil words written on the paper:

"You don't want me to get sick and want me to take medicine, how can I bear to let you travel back and forth? Smile."
